```sql
	   ,t.PnL_CFD_Stocks_LevCFD
	   ,t.PnL_Real_Crypto_Lev1
	   ,t.PnL_CFD_Crypto_LevCFD
	   ,t.IsFunded_New
	   ,t.Active_FX
	   ,t.Active_Comm
	   ,t.Active_Ind
	   ,t.ActiveOpen_FX
	   ,t.ActiveOpen_Comm
	   ,t.ActiveOpen_Ind
	   ,t.Revenue_FX
	   ,t.Revenue_Comm
	   ,t.Revenue_Ind
	   ,t.PnL_FX
	   ,t.PnL_Comm
	   ,t.PnL_Ind
	   ,t.UpdateDate
           ,t.EOW_LSD	 
,CASE WHEN t.EOW_Club IN ('LowBronze','HighBronze') THEN 'Bronze' ELSE t.EOW_Club END AS EOW_Club_New
,LAG(t.IsFunded_New,1) OVER (PARTITION BY t.CID ORDER BY FirstDayOfWeek) AS Lag_IsEOM_Funded_NEW
,bdcd.FirstNewFundedDate
,ISNULL(bdcd.Gender,'M') Gender
,CASE WHEN t.ActiveOpen_Real_Stocks + t.ActiveOpen_CFD_Stocks > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ActiveOpen_Stocks
,CASE WHEN t.ActiveOpen_Real_Crypto + t.ActiveOpen_CFD_Crypto > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ActiveOpen_Crypto
,t.Revenue_Real_Stocks + t.Revenue_CFD_Stocks AS Revenue_Stocks
,t.Revenue_Real_Crypto + t.Revenue_CFD_Crypto AS Revenue_Crypto
,t.NewTrades_Real_Stocks + t.NewTrades_CFD_Stocks AS NewTrades_Stocks
,t.NewTrades_Real_Crypto + t.NewTrades_CFD_Crypto AS NewTrades_Crypto
,Cluster.ClusterDetail
,DATEDIFF(DAY,bdcd.FirstNewFundedDate,DATEADD(DAY,6, t.FirstDayOfWeek)) AS SeniorityFunded
,nm.CFD_Status AS Negative_Market_Status_Curr,
       CAST(CASE WHEN nm.CFD_Status = 'CFD_Blocked' THEN 'Yes' ELSE 'No' END AS CHAR) AS IsCFDBlocked_Curr,
       CASE WHEN nm.CFD_Status = 'CFD_Allowed' AND ISNULL(nm.BlockDate, '1900-01-01') > '1900-01-01' THEN 'CFD_Allowed_were_Blocked' 
       ELSE nm.CFD_Status 
       END AS Negative_Market_Status_Include_H,
       CAST(CASE 
           WHEN (nm.CFD_Status = 'CFD_Allowed' AND ISNULL(nm.BlockDate, '1900-01-01') > '1900-01-01') OR nm.CFD_Status = 'CFD_Blocked' THEN 'Blocked' 
           ELSE 'NotBlocked' 
       END AS CHAR) AS IsCFDBlocked_Include_H



,  CASE  
             WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Affiliate%' THEN 'Affiliate'
		     WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Direct%' THEN 'Direct'
			 WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Friend Referral%' THEN 'Friend Referral'
			 WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Media Performance%' THEN 'Media Performance'
		     WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Media Programmatic%' THEN 'Media Programmatic'
			 WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%Mobile Acquisition%' THEN 'Mobile Acquisition'
			 WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%SEM%' THEN 'SEM'
			 WHEN bdcd.Channel LIKE '%SEO%' THEN 'SEO'
		ELSE 'Other' END AS Channel_Group ,
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) <= 24 THEN '18-24'  
                  WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 25 AND 34 THEN '25-34'  
                  WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 35 AND 44 THEN '35-44'  
                  WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 45 AND 54 THEN '45-54'  
                  WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) >= 55 THEN '55+'  
                  ELSE NULL END AS Age_Group


from BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_WeeklyPanel_FullData t with (nolock)
JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CIDFirstDates bdcd with (nolock)
ON t.CID = bdcd.CID 
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Country] dc1 WITH (NOLOCK)
ON t.Country = dc1.Name
LEFT JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_Scored_Appropriateness_Negative_Market nm on t.CID = nm.RealCID

LEFT JOIN (
SELECT bdcdc.CID
,bdcdc.ClusterDetail
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_DailyCluster bdcdc 
WHERE bdcdc.ToDateID = 99991231
) AS Cluster
ON t.CID = Cluster.CID
WHERE t.FirstDayOfWeek >= cast(DateAdd(wk, DateDiff(wk, -1, GetDate()) -11, -1) AS DATE)
and t.FirstDayOfWeek <= cast(DateAdd(wk, DateDiff(wk, -1, GetDate()) -1, -1) AS DATE)
--AND SSWeekNumberOfYear <>1
```

### 133. BI_DB_FirstDates

- Tableau id: `eb325dca-1c53-a7bb-f59c-f08a9b1b6dd7`

```sql
SELECT fd.CID
	  ,fd.Club
	  ,fd.Country
	  ,fd.Region
	  ,fd.Verified
	  ,fd.DocsOK
	  ,fd.registered
	  ,fd.Manager
	  ,fd.FirstDepositDate
	  ,fd.VerificationLevel1Date
	  ,fd.VerificationLevel2Date
	  ,fd.VerificationLevel3Date
	  ,fd.EvMatchStatusDate
	  ,fd.EvMatchStatus
	  ,fd.FirstPosOpenDate FirstAction
,dr.Name Regulation
FROM [BI_DB].[dbo].[BI_DB_CIDFirstDates] fd WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT JOIN DWH.dbo.Dim_Regulation dr WITH (NOLOCK)
ON fd.RegulationID=dr.ID
WHERE fd.registered >='2021-01-01 00:00:00.000'
```

### 134. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f0e5bd4e-8228-cff1-2e0f-a2bae6d920de`

```sql
select
dc.RealCID,
dc.GCID,
aty.Name as AccountType,
pl.Name as ClubLevel,
dc.FunnelID,
dc.FunnelFromID,
CASE  WHEN FunnelFromID=65 THEN 'From SMSF Funnel'WHEN aty.Name IN ('SMSF') THEN aty.Name end as [SMSF/FromSMSFfunnel],
dc.RegisteredReal as RegDate,
dc.FirstDepositDate,
fd.FirstDepositAmount,
MAX(CA.FirstOccurred) as FirstActionDate,
dc.VerificationLevelID,
dc.AffiliateID ,
dm.FirstName + ' ' + dm.LastName as AccountManager,
dr.Name as Regulaiton,
dc.Zip,
dc.City,
datediff(year,dc.BirthDate,getdate()) as Age,
v.Liabilities + v.ActualNWA AS TotalEquity ,
DESK.CFDesk as Desk
from DWH_dbo.Dim_Customer dc
left join DWH_dbo.Dim_AccountType aty on aty.AccountTypeID=dc.AccountTypeID
left join DWH_dbo.Dim_Regulation dr on dr.ID=dc.RegulationID
left join [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CIDFirstDates] fd on fd.CID=dc.RealCID
LEFT JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Manager dm on dm.ManagerID=dc.AccountManagerID
LEFT JOIN DWH_dbo.Fact_FirstCustomerAction CA ON CA.RealCID=dc.RealCID
left join DWH_dbo.Dim_PlayerLevel pl on pl.PlayerLevelID=dc.PlayerLevelID
left join  DWH_dbo.Dim_Desk DESK ON DESK.CountryID=dc.CountryID AND DESK.LanguageID=dc.LanguageID
left join DWH_dbo.V_Liabilities v on v.CID=dc.RealCID and v.DateID=CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), GETDATE()-1, 112)
where dc.AccountTypeID=14--SMSF
OR dc.FunnelFromID=65
group by 
dc.RealCID,
dc.GCID,
pl.Name,
aty.Name,
dc.FunnelID,
dc.RegisteredReal ,
dc.FirstDepositDate,
fd.FirstDepositAmount,
dc.VerificationLevelID,
dc.AffiliateID ,
dm.FirstName + ' ' + dm.LastName ,
dr.Name,
dc.Zip,
dc.City,
datediff(year,dc.BirthDate,getdate()) ,
DESK.CFDesk,
v.Liabilities + v.ActualNWA,
dc.FunnelFromID,
CASE WHEN aty.Name IN ('SMSF') THEN aty.Name WHEN FunnelFromID=65 THEN 'From SMSF Funnel' end
```

### 137. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f55c0920-fc6a-fd53-066d-8c54a5e4e3d1`

```sql
SELECT pan.[CID]
, dc.FirstName + ' ' + dc.LastName AS ClientName
, [fd].[Manager]
, [fd].[Club]
, [fd].[RealizedEquity]
, (CASE WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 5000 THEN 5000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 10000 THEN 10000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 25000 THEN 25000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 50000 THEN 50000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 250000 THEN 250000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] >= 250000 THEN NULL
END) AS AmountBelowUpgradeThreshold
, (CASE WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 5000 THEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] / 5000.0
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 10000 THEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] / 10000.0
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 25000 THEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] / 25000.0
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 50000 THEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] / 50000.0
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 250000 THEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] / 250000.0
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] >= 250000 THEN NULL
END) AS PercentageOfUpgradeThreshold
, fd.[LastContactDate]
, DATEDIFF(HOUR, fd.[LastContactDate], GETDATE()) / 24.0 AS DaysSinceLastContact
, SUM(CASE WHEN [pan].[ActiveDate] >= DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, GETDATE()) -3, 0) THEN pan.Revenue_Total END) AS RevenueLast3FullMonths
, SUM(CASE WHEN [pan].[ActiveDate] = DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, GETDATE()) -1, 0) THEN pan.Revenue_Total END) AS RevenueLastMonth
, SUM(CASE WHEN [pan].[ActiveDate] = DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, GETDATE()), 0) THEN pan.Revenue_Total END) AS RevenueThisMonth
FROM [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData] pan WITH (NOLOCK)
JOIN [DWH_dbo].Dim_Customer dc WITH (NOLOCK) ON pan.CID = dc.RealCID
JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Country] dc1 ON dc1.CountryID = dc.CountryID
LEFT JOIN [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CIDFirstDates] fd WITH (NOLOCK) ON fd.CID = dc.[RealCID]
WHERE [pan].[ActiveDate] >= DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, GETDATE()) -3, 0)
AND dc1.[Region] = 'UK' AND [dc].[IsValidCustomer] = 1 AND [fd].[Club] IN ('Gold', 'Platinum', 'Platinum Plus', 'Diamond') --AND [pan].[CID] = 3711653
GROUP BY pan.[CID]
, dc.FirstName + ' ' + dc.LastName
, [fd].[Manager]
, [fd].[Club]
, [fd].[RealizedEquity]
, (CASE WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 5000 THEN 5000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 10000 THEN 10000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 25000 THEN 25000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 50000 THEN 50000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
WHEN [fd].[RealizedEquity] < 250000 THEN 250000 - [fd].[RealizedEquity]
END)
, fd.[LastContactDate]
, DATEDIFF(HOUR, fd.[LastContactDate], GETDATE()) / 24.0
```

### 139. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f6481890-31c8-5d7c-1faf-2e100c3378f4`

```sql
select    bdduftp.* , 
 (DATEPART(WEEKDAY, Date) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7 + 1 AS WeekdayNum,
           daff.Contact,
	       dc.MarketingRegionManualName,
	 	   bdkscl.Cluster,
		   ffa.FirstInstrument, 
		   YEAR(bdcd.registered) AS RegisteredYear,
           CAST(bdcd.FirstDepositAmount AS INT) FTDA,
		   plt.FTDPlatformName AS FTDPlatform,
           CASE WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) <= 24 THEN '18-24'  
                WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 25 AND 34 THEN '25-34'  
                WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 35 AND 44 THEN '35-44'  
                WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) BETWEEN 45 AND 54 THEN '45-54'  
                WHEN FLOOR(DATEDIFF(DAY, bdcd.BirthDate, GETDATE()) / 365.25) >= 55 THEN '55+'  
                ELSE NULL END AS Age_Group,
                GETDATE() as DateU 
		  
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DepositUsersFirstTouchPoints bdduftp
JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CIDFirstDates  bdcd                        ON bdduftp.CID = bdcd.CID
JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Customer as dmmc                               ON bdduftp.CID = dmmc.RealCID
LEFT JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_FTDPlatform AS plt                        ON plt.FTDPlatformID = dmmc.FTDPlatformID
LEFT JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Country  dc                               ON dc.Name=bdduftp.Country
LEFT JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_KYC_Score_CID_Level bdkscl            ON bdkscl.RealCID = bdduftp.CID
LEFT JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_First5Actions	ffa                     ON bdduftp.CID = ffa.CID
LEFT JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Affiliate daff                            ON daff.AffiliateID = bdduftp.AffiliateID

WHERE  bdduftp.Date>=CAST(Dateadd(Month,Datediff(Month, 0, DATEADD(m, -6,GETDATE())), 0) AS DATE)
AND bdcd.Region <> 'Unknown'
AND bdduftp.Date <= getdate()-1
```

### 140. Custom SQL Query1

- Tableau id: `f6edf665-1e96-aa66-47ce-51e397cfd9e6`

```sql
SELECT ISNULL(costfinance.YearMonth, LTV_Data.YearMonth)YearMonth,
       ISNULL(costfinance.Channel, LTV_Data.Channel)Channel,
	   ISNULL(costfinance.Region, LTV_Data.Region)Region,
	   LTV_Data.FTDs,
	   LTV_Data.LTV,
	   LTV_Data.LTV_FTDs,
	   costfinance.Cost,
	   leadscore.LTV_LeadScore,
	   leadscore.Users_LeadScore
FROM (SELECT CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),dc.FirstDepositDate,126) YearMonth,
             CASE WHEN dc1.SubChannel='FB' THEN 'Facebook'
      	          WHEN dc1.SubChannel='ASA' THEN 'ASA'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Twitter' THEN 'Twitter'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Outbrain' THEN 'Outbrain'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Taboola' THEN 'Taboola'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Media Performance') THEN 'Media Performance'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Media Programmatic' THEN 'Media Programmatic'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Mobile Non-CPA','Mobile CPA') THEN 'Mobile'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SMM','Direct','Direct Mobile') THEN 'Direct'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Google Brand','Google Search','Google UAC','YT') THEN 'Google'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SEM Other','Bing Search') THEN 'SEM'
				  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Discovery') THEN 'Google'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('IBs','Affiliate') THEN 'Affiliate'
      	     ELSE dc1.Channel END Channel,
      	     dc2.MarketingRegionManualName Region,
			 COUNT(dc.RealCID) FTDs,
             SUM(ltv.LTV_8Y_VolFix) LTV,
      	     COUNT(ltv.RealCID) LTV_FTDs
      FROM DWH_dbo.Dim_Customer dc
      LEFT JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_LTV_Predictions ltv ON dc.RealCID=ltv.RealCID AND dc.IsValidCustomer=1
      JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Channel dc1 ON dc.SubChannelID = dc1.SubChannelID
      JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Country dc2 ON dc.CountryID = dc2.CountryID
      WHERE YEAR(dc.FirstDepositDate)>=2023
	  AND dc.IsValidCustomer = 1
      GROUP BY CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),dc.FirstDepositDate,126),
               CASE WHEN dc1.SubChannel='FB' THEN 'Facebook'
      	            WHEN dc1.SubChannel='ASA' THEN 'ASA'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Twitter' THEN 'Twitter'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Outbrain' THEN 'Outbrain'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Taboola' THEN 'Taboola'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Media Performance') THEN 'Media Performance'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Media Programmatic' THEN 'Media Programmatic'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Mobile Non-CPA','Mobile CPA') THEN 'Mobile'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SMM','Direct','Direct Mobile') THEN 'Direct'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Google Brand','Google Search','Google UAC','YT') THEN 'Google'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SEM Other','Bing Search') THEN 'SEM'
					WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Discovery') THEN 'Google'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('IBs','Affiliate') THEN 'Affiliate'
      	       ELSE dc1.Channel END,
      			dc2.MarketingRegionManualName) LTV_Data
FULL OUTER JOIN (SELECT [month] YearMonth,
                        channel Channel,
	                    region Region,
	                    cost Cost
                 FROM [BI_DB_dbo].[External_Fivetran_gsheet_costfinance]) costfinance ON costfinance.YearMonth=LTV_Data.YearMonth
				                                                                          AND costfinance.Channel COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS=LTV_Data.Channel COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS
																						  AND costfinance.Region COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS=LTV_Data.Region COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS
																						 



LEFT JOIN (SELECT bdc.NewMarketingRegion Region,
                  bdc.Channel,
                  SUM(bdlp.LTV_8Y_VolFix) LTV_LeadScore,
                  COUNT(scl.RealCID) Users_LeadScore
           FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_KYC_Score_CID_Level scl
		   JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CIDFirstDates bdc ON scl.RealCID=bdc.CID AND bdc.FirstDepositDate IS NOT NULL
           JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_LTV_Predictions  bdlp ON scl.RealCID = bdlp.RealCID AND bdlp.LTV_8Y_VolFix IS NOT NULL
           WHERE CAST(bdc.FirstDepositDate AS DATE) >=DATEADD(MONTH,-7,CAST(CONCAT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),GETDATE(),126),'-01') AS DATE)) 
		     AND scl.Cluster!='No Cluster'
           GROUP BY bdc.NewMarketingRegion, bdc.Channel) leadscore ON LTV_Data.Region=leadscore.Region AND LTV_Data.Channel=leadscore.Channel
```

### 141. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f8732718-0a67-56a4-4117-a1b261cbce80`

```sql
SELECT
	pan.CID
   ,pan.FTD_Month
   ,pan.FirstAction
   ,pan.Country
   ,pan.[Region]
   ,[dc].[City]

   , (CASE WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('ne', 'ca', 'dh', 'sr', 'ts', 'dl') THEN 'North East' 
  WHEN (lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('la', 'fy', 'pr', 'bb', 'hx', 'ol', 'bl', 'wn', 'la', 'wa', 'sk', 'cw', 'im') OR lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,1)) = 'm') THEN 'North West' 
  WHEN (lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('bd', 'hg', 'ls', 'wf', 'hd', 'dn', 'hu', 'yo') OR lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,1)) = 's') THEN 'Yorkshire & Humber' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('de', 'ng', 'ln', 'le', 'nn', 'ox', 'hp', 'rg') THEN 'East Midlands' 
  WHEN (lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('st', 'tf', 'wv', 'ws', 'dy', 'cv', 'wr', 'hr') OR lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,1)) = 'b') THEN 'West Midlands' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('pe', 'nr', 'ip', 'mk', 'sg', 'cb', 'co', 'cm', 'lu') THEN 'East of England' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('gu','rh','bn','tn','me','ct') THEN 'South West' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('gl', 'bs', 'sn', 'ba', 'sp', 'so ', 'po', 'bh', 'dt', 'ta', 'ex', 'tq ', 'pl', 'tr') THEN 'South East' 
  WHEN (lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('wc', 'ec', 'sw', 'sw', 'nw', 'se', 'ss', 'rm', 'da', 'br', 'ig', 'cr', 'sm', 'kt', 'tw', 'sl', 'ub', 'ha', 'wd', 'al', 'en') OR lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,1)) IN ('n','w', 'e')) THEN 'London' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('ll','ch','sy','ld','sa','cf','np') THEN 'Wales' 
  WHEN (lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) IN ('dg','td','eh','ml','ka','pa','fk','ky','ph','dd','ab','iv','kw','ze') OR lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,1)) = 'g') THEN 'Scotland' 
  WHEN lower(substring(REPLACE(dc.Zip, ' ', ''),1,2)) = 'bt' THEN 'East Midlands' 
  ELSE 'N/A' END) AS RegionInUK

   ,fd.Manager
   ,fd.Club
   ,pan.Active_Month RevenueMonth
   ,[Revenue_Total]
   ,fd.RealizedEquity
   ,dcl.ClusterDetail

FROM [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData] pan WITH (NOLOCK)
LEFT JOIN [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CIDFirstDates] fd WITH (NOLOCK)
	ON fd.CID = pan.CID
LEFT JOIN [BI_DB_dbo].[BI_DB_CID_DailyCluster] dcl WITH (NOLOCK)
	ON pan.CID = dcl.CID
		AND dcl.IsLastCluster = 1
JOIN [DWH_dbo].Dim_Customer dc WITH (NOLOCK)
	ON pan.CID = dc.RealCID
WHERE pan.Region IN ('UK', 'German')
AND pan.ActiveDate >= DATEADD(MONTH, -4, GETDATE())
AND [Revenue_Total] >= 10
```

### 142. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f970877f-5948-f55b-c63f-cacf73f1d64d`

```sql
SELECT 

concat(case 
	when c.AccountTypeID = 2 then 1 
	when c.AccountTypeID = 15 then 1 
	else 2
	end
	,';'
	,z.TIN_Value
	,';'
	,
c.FirstName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI, ' '
,c.LastName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI
,
';') as 'column'
,case 
	when c.AccountTypeID = 2 then 1 
	when c.AccountTypeID = 15 then 1 
	else 2
	end as 'val'
,c.RealCID
,z.TIN_Value
,concat(
c.FirstName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI, ' '
,c.LastName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI
) as 'name'
,c.RegulationID
,c.VerificationLevelID
,c.RegisteredReal
,d.VerificationLevel2Date
,concat(left(z.TIN_Value,5),c.LastName) as '5SSNLastName'

--into #US
  from [DWH].[dbo].[Dim_Customer] c 

  left join [BI_DB].[dbo].[BI_DB_CIDFirstDates] d 
  on d.CID = c.RealCID



  left join [BI_DB].[dbo].[BI_DB_Tax_Compliance_TIN] z 
  on c.GCID = z.GCID
  and z.FieldID = 6

  where 
  c.CountryID = 219 
  --and len(z.TIN_Value) = 9 --only take 9 digit values
  --and len(concat(c.FirstName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI, ' '
--,c.LastName collate SQL_Latin1_General_CP1253_CI_AI
--)) <= 40
 and c.VerificationLevelID >= 2 --level 2 or higher
 and d.VerificationLevel2Date >= '2021-01-01'
```

### 144. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `fbad34b2-76ce-3068-ca69-d3cc16468bcd`

```sql
SELECT ISNULL(costfinance.YearMonth, LTV_Data.YearMonth)YearMonth,
       ISNULL(costfinance.Channel, LTV_Data.Channel)Channel,
	   ISNULL(costfinance.Region, LTV_Data.Region)Region,
	   LTV_Data.FTDs,
	   LTV_Data.LTV,
	   LTV_Data.LTV_FTDs,
	   costfinance.Cost,
	   leadscore.LTV_LeadScore,
	   leadscore.Users_LeadScore
FROM (SELECT CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),dc.FirstDepositDate,126) YearMonth,
             CASE WHEN dc1.SubChannel='FB' THEN 'Facebook'
      	          WHEN dc1.SubChannel='ASA' THEN 'ASA'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Twitter' THEN 'Twitter'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Outbrain' THEN 'Outbrain'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Taboola' THEN 'Taboola'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Media Performance') THEN 'Media Performance'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Media Programmatic' THEN 'Media Programmatic'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Mobile Non-CPA','Mobile CPA') THEN 'Mobile'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SMM','Direct','Direct Mobile') THEN 'Direct'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Google Brand','Google Search','Google UAC','YT') THEN 'Google'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SEM Other','Bing Search') THEN 'SEM'
				  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Discovery') THEN 'Google'
      			  WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('IBs','Affiliate') THEN 'Affiliate'
      	     ELSE dc1.Channel END Channel,
      	     dc2.MarketingRegionManualName Region,
			 COUNT(dc.RealCID) FTDs,
             SUM(ltv.Revenue8Y_LTV_New) LTV,
      	     COUNT(ltv.CID) LTV_FTDs
      FROM DWH_dbo.Dim_Customer dc
      LEFT JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_LTV_BI_Actual ltv ON dc.RealCID=ltv.CID AND dc.IsValidCustomer=1
      JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Channel dc1 ON dc.SubChannelID = dc1.SubChannelID
      JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Country dc2 ON dc.CountryID = dc2.CountryID
      WHERE YEAR(dc.FirstDepositDate)>=2023
	  AND dc.IsValidCustomer = 1
      GROUP BY CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),dc.FirstDepositDate,126),
               CASE WHEN dc1.SubChannel='FB' THEN 'Facebook'
      	            WHEN dc1.SubChannel='ASA' THEN 'ASA'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Twitter' THEN 'Twitter'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Outbrain' THEN 'Outbrain'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Taboola' THEN 'Taboola'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Media Performance') THEN 'Media Performance'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel='Media Programmatic' THEN 'Media Programmatic'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Mobile Non-CPA','Mobile CPA') THEN 'Mobile'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SMM','Direct','Direct Mobile') THEN 'Direct'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Google Brand','Google Search','Google UAC','YT') THEN 'Google'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('SEM Other','Bing Search') THEN 'SEM'
					WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('Discovery') THEN 'Google'
      			    WHEN dc1.SubChannel IN ('IBs','Affiliate') THEN 'Affiliate'
      	       ELSE dc1.Channel END,
      			dc2.MarketingRegionManualName) LTV_Data
FULL OUTER JOIN (SELECT [month] YearMonth,
                        channel Channel,
	                    region Region,
	                    cost Cost
                 FROM [BI_DB_dbo].[External_Fivetran_gsheet_costfinance]) costfinance 
				 ON costfinance.YearMonth=LTV_Data.YearMonth
				 AND costfinance.Channel COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS=LTV_Data.Channel COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS
				 AND costfinance.Region COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS=LTV_Data.Region COLLATE Latin1_General_CS_AS
																						 
LEFT JOIN (SELECT bdc.NewMarketingRegion Region,
                  bdc.Channel,
                  SUM(bdlp.Revenue8Y_LTV_New) LTV_LeadScore,
                  COUNT(scl.RealCID) Users_LeadScore
           FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_KYC_Score_CID_Level scl
		   JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CIDFirstDates bdc ON scl.RealCID=bdc.CID AND bdc.FirstDepositDate IS NOT NULL
           JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_LTV_BI_Actual  bdlp ON scl.RealCID = bdlp.CID AND bdlp.Revenue8Y_LTV_New IS NOT NULL
           WHERE CAST(bdc.FirstDepositDate AS DATE) >=DATEADD(MONTH,-7,CAST(CONCAT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7),GETDATE(),126),'-01') AS DATE)) 
		     AND scl.Cluster!='No Cluster'
           GROUP BY bdc.NewMarketingRegion, bdc.Channel) leadscore ON LTV_Data.Region=leadscore.Region AND LTV_Data.Channel=leadscore.Channel
```

### 145. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `ffe3282f-2058-8e91-ecec-e2240711e7e1`

```sql
SELECT DISTINCT mp.CID
		,mp.ActiveDate
		,mp.EOM_Club
                ,mp.AccountManager
		,mp.ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual
		,mp.EOM_Balance AvailableBalance
		,bdcd.LastPosOpenDate
		,mp.Country
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData mp
JOIN [BI_DB_dbo].[External_Fivetran_google_sheets_account_manager_targets_2024] t 
ON t.account_manager = mp.AccountManager
JOIN BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CIDFirstDates bdcd
ON mp.CID = bdcd.CID
WHERE  mp.ActiveDate = (SELECT MAX(mp1.ActiveDate) FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData mp1)
AND mp.EOM_Club IN ('Diamond','Platinum Plus')
```

  - [Dashboard 1](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/UnfundedLevel3Verifiedclients/Dashboard1)
- **Verification Status ** (Verifications)
  - [Verification Status Per Month ](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/VerificationStatus/VerificationStatusPerMonth_1)
  - [Verification Status Per Country Per Month ](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/VerificationStatus/VerificationStatusPerCountryPerMonth_1)
  - [Verification Status per Country ](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/VerificationStatus/VerificationStatusperCountry_1)
- **Instruments Volume** (Volatility Alerts)
  - [MTD Positions.](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/InstrumentsVolume/MTDPositions_)
  - [Comparison %MoM](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/InstrumentsVolume/ComparisonMoM)
  - [Instrument (D)](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/InstrumentsVolume/InstrumentD)
  - [Instrument (m)](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/InstrumentsVolume/Instrumentm)
- **KPIs Monitoring** (📊 Core Monitoring)
  - [KPIs Monitoring](https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/KPIsMonitoring/KPIsMonitoring)

## Downstream calculated fields (in embedded datasources)

### Workbook: Acquirers' Performance Dashboard

#### Datasource: All Deposits Tracking

- **%Approved**

  ```
  SUM([Approved_Deposits])/COUNT([DepositID])
  ```

- **%PaymentApproval**

  ```
  SUM([Approved])/SUM([_Try])
  ```

- **Approved_Deposits**

  ```
  IF [PaymentStatus]='Approved' then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **BankNameGroup**

  ```
  IF CONTAINS(LOWER([BankName]), "revolut") THEN "Revolut"
  ELSE "Other"
  END
  ```

- **calc,TryWeek**

  ```
  SUM([_Try])
  /
  SUM({ FIXED [Week_] : SUM([_Try]) })
  ```

- **Choose KPI**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI]
  WHEN '%PaymentApproval' THEN [%PaymentApproval]
  WHEN '_Try' THEN sum([_Try])
  WHEN 'Approved' THEN sum([Approved])
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheet_#_AllDeposits**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI]
  WHEN '_Try' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Approved' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheet_%_AllDeposits**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI]
  WHEN '%PaymentApproval' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **Split By.**

  ```
  CASE [Split By]
      WHEN 'Country' THEN [Country]
      WHEN 'NewMarketingRegion' THEN [NewMarketingRegion]
      WHEN 'FundingType' THEN [FundingType]
      WHEN 'DepositType' THEN [DepositType]
   WHEN 'Provider' THEN [Provider]
   WHEN 'BankName' THEN [BankName]
   WHEN 'BankNameGroup' THEN [BankNameGroup]
   WHEN 'CarTypeName' THEN [CarTypeName]
   WHEN 'Currency' THEN [Currency]
      ELSE ''
  END
  ```

#### Datasource: FTDs Split - Global FTD

- **.SplitBy_Global**

  ```
  CASE [Split By_Global]
      WHEN 'Country' THEN [Country]
      WHEN 'Region' THEN [Region]
      WHEN 'FundingType' THEN [FundingType]
      WHEN 'FTDPlatformName' THEN [FTDPlatformName]
      ELSE ''
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheetW**

  ```
  CASE   [ChooseTimeFrame]
  WHEN 'Week' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **Weekend**

  ```
  IF [WeekdayNum] IN (6,7) THEN 'Weekend'
  ELSE 'Weekday'
  END
  ```

#### Datasource: Funnel Deposit Attempts

- **%DepositTryV2**

  ```
  SUM([V2toDepositTrySameWeek])/SUM([V2])
  ```

- **%DepositTryV3**

  ```
  SUM([V3toDepositTrySameWeek])/SUM([V3])
  ```

- **%FirstDepSuccessfromV2**

  ```
  SUM([Approved_V2toDepositTrySameWeek])/SUM(V2toDepositTrySameWeek)
  ```

- **%FirstDepSuccessfromV3**

  ```
  SUM([Approved_V3toDepositTrySameWeek])/SUM(V3toDepositTrySameWeek)
  ```

- **Choose KPI_Funnel**

  ```
  CASE [Choose KPI_Funnel]
  WHEN '%DepositTryV2' THEN [%DepositTryV2]
  WHEN '%DepositTryV3' THEN [%DepositTryV3]
  WHEN '%FirstDepSuccessfromV2' THEN [%FirstDepSuccessfromV2]
  WHEN '%FirstDepSuccessfromV3' THEN [%FirstDepSuccessfromV3]
  WHEN '#TriesfromV2' THEN SUM([V2toDepositTrySameWeek])
  WHEN '#TriesfromV3' THEN SUM([V3toDepositTrySameWeek])
  WHEN '#SuccessfromV2' THEN SUM([Approved_V2toDepositTrySameWeek])
  WHEN '#SuccessfromV3' THEN SUM([Approved_V3toDepositTrySameWeek])
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheetV2#**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI_Funnel]
  WHEN '#TriesfromV2' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN '#SuccessfromV2' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheetV2%**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI_Funnel]
  WHEN '%DepositTryV2' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN '%FirstDepSuccessfromV2' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheetV3#**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI_Funnel]
  WHEN '#TriesfromV3' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN '#SuccessfromV3' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **ShowSheetV3%**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI_Funnel]
  WHEN '%DepositTryV3' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN '%FirstDepSuccessfromV3' THEN 'TRUE'
  WHEN 'Test' THEN 'TRUE'
  END
  ```

- **Split By_Funnel.**

  ```
  CASE [Split By_Funnel]
      WHEN 'CountryName' THEN [CountryName]
      WHEN 'MarketingRegion' THEN [MarketingRegion]
      WHEN 'Channel' THEN [Channel]
      WHEN 'SubChannel' THEN [SubChannel]
      WHEN 'FundingType' THEN [FundingType]
      WHEN 'CarTypeName' THEN [CarTypeName]
      WHEN 'Currency' THEN [Currency]
      ELSE ''
  END
  ```

- **Switch_**

  ```
  IF [Choose KPI_Funnel] IN (1, 3) THEN 'V2'
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI_Funnel] IN (2, 4) THEN 'V3'
  END
  ```

### Workbook: Acquisition Monthly Dashboard

#### Datasource: CFO Dashboard-Data (local copy)

- **% Change From Last 12 Months**

  ```
  SUM([Last Month KPI])/([Avg 12 Months KPI])-1
  ```

- **% change from last 8 weeks choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last week KPI])/([Last 8 week Avg KPI])-1
  ```

- **% Change from Prev Month**

  ```
  SUM([Last Month KPI])/SUM([Prev Month KPI])-1
  ```

- **% change from Prev week choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last week KPI])/SUM([Prev week KPI])-1
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Demo-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([Demo-FTD],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Demo-FTD],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: DeppAtt-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([DeppAtt-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([DeppAtt-FTD],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([DeppAtt-FTD],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: FirstCross-First Action-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([First Action-First Cross]-WINDOW_AVG([First Action-First Cross],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([First Action-First Cross],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: FirstDemoTrade-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstDemoTrade])-WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstDemoTrade]),-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstDemoTrade]),-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: FirstNewFunded-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded])-WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstNewFunded]),-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstNewFunded]),-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: FTD-FirstAction-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([FTD-FirstAction]-WINDOW_AVG([FTD-FirstAction],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([FTD-FirstAction],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: FTDs-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([FTD])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([FTD]),-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([FTD]),-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Reg-Demo-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-Demo]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-Demo],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-Demo],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Reg-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-FTD],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-FTD],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Reg-NewFunded-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-New Funded]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-New Funded],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-New Funded],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Reg-V1-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-V1]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-V1],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-V1],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: Regs-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([Registration])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([Registration]),-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([Registration]),-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: SecondAction-FirstAction-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([FirstAction-SecondAction]-WINDOW_AVG([FirstAction-SecondAction],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([FirstAction-SecondAction],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: V1-V2-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V1-V2]-WINDOW_AVG([V1-V2],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V1-V2],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Months: V2-V3-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V2-V3]-WINDOW_AVG([V2-V3],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V2-V3],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 12 Moths: V3-DeppAtt-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V3-DeppAtt]-WINDOW_AVG([V3-DeppAtt],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V3-DeppAtt],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG 8 Weeks-ABS-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([Chosen KPI])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-8,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-8,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG-ABS-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen KPI],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Chosen KPI],-12,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG-CVR-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen CVR KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-12,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-12,-1)
  ```

- **%Change 12 Months CVR KPIs**

  ```
  [CVR KPI Last Month]-[CVR KPI 12 Months]
  ```

- **%Change Prev Month CVR KPIs**

  ```
  [CVR KPI Last Month]-[CVR KPI Prev Month]
  ```

- **0**

  ```
  0
  ```

- **12 Months diff from AVG-CVR-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen CVR KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-12,-1))
  ```

- **Avg 12 Months KPI**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 12 months] THEN [Chosen KPI] END)/12
  ```

- **avg.FTDA**

  ```
  sum([Unique_FTDA])/SUM([FTD])
  ```

- **avgLTV**

  ```
  [LTV]
  ```

- **Chosen CVR KPI**

  ```
  case [Choose CVR KPI]
  when 'Reg-Demo' THEN [Reg-Demo]
  when 'Demo-FTD' then  [Demo-FTD]
  when 'Reg-V1' then  [Reg-V1]
  when 'V1-V2' then  [V1-V2]
  when 'V2-V3' then  [V2-V3]
  when 'V3-DeppAtt' then  [V3-DeppAtt]
  when 'DeppAtt-FTD' then  [DeppAtt-FTD]
  when 'Reg-FTD' then  [Reg-FTD]
  when 'Reg-NewFunded' then  [Reg-New Funded]
  when 'FTD-FirstAction' then  [FTD-FirstAction]
  when 'FirstAction-SecondAction' then  [FirstAction-SecondAction]
  when 'FirstAction-FirstCross' then  [First Action-First Cross]
  END
  ```

- **Chosen CVR KPI 12 Months**

  ```
  case [Choose CVR KPI]

  when 'Demo-FTD' then  [Demo-FTD Last 12 Months]

  when 'Reg-FTD' then  [Reg-FTD Last 12 Months]
  when 'Reg-NewFunded' then  [Reg-NewFunded Last 12 Months]
  when 'FTD-FirstAction' then  [FTD-FirstAction Last 12 Months]
  when 'FirstAction-SecondAction' then  [FirstAction-SecondAction Last 12 Months]
  ```

  ```
  END
  ```

- **Chosen KPI**

  ```
  CASE [Choose KPI]
  WHEN 'FTD' THEN [FTD]
  WHEN 'Registrations' then  [Registration]
  WHEN 'FirstDemoTrade' then  [FirstDemoTrade]
  WHEN 'FirstNewFunded' then  [FirstNewFunded]
  WHEN 'V1' then [VerificationLevel1]
  WHEN 'V2' then  [VerificationLevel2]
  WHEN 'V3' then  [VerificationLevel3]
  WHEN 'FirstAction' then  [FirstAction]
  WHEN 'SecondAction' then [SecondAction]
  WHEN 'FirstCross' then [FirstCross] 
  WHEN 'Unique_FTDA' then [Unique_FTDA] 
  WHEN 'avgLTV' THEN [LTV]
  
  END
  ```

- **Chosen KPI-AVG 12 Months-AVG WIN**

  ```
  WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-12,-1)
  ```

- **Chosen KPI_agg**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI]
  
  WHEN 'avgLTV' THEN  SUM([LTV]) / SUM([ltvusers])
  
  END
  ```

- **Current month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = DATETRUNC('month',TODAY())
  ```

- **Current Week **

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = DATETRUNC('week',TODAY())
  ```

- **CVR KPI 12 Months**

  ```
  case [Choose CVR KPI- Same Month]
  when 'Reg-Demo' THEN [Reg-Demo 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'Demo-FTD' then  [Demo-FTD 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'Reg-V1' then  [Reg-V1 Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'V1-V2' then  [V1-V2 Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'V2-V3' then  [V2-V3 Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'V3-DeppAtt' then  [V3-DeppAtt Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'DeppAtt-FTD' then  [DeppAtt-FTD Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'Reg-FTD' then  [Reg-FTD Last 12 Months Same Month] 
  when 'V2-FTD' then [V2-FTD Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'V3-FTD' then [V3-FTD Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'Reg-NewFunded' then  [Reg-NewFunded Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'FTD-FirstAction' then  [FTD-FirstAction 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'FTD-New Funded' then [FTD-new funded 5 months same month]
  when 'FirstAction-SecondAction' then  [FirstAction-SecondAction Last 12 Months Same Month]
  when 'FirstAction-FirstCross' then  [FirstAction-FirstCross Last 12 Months Same Month]
  END
  ```

  ```
  when 'V2-FTD' then [V2-FTD Last Month Same Month]
  when 'V3-FTD' then [V3-FTD Last Month Same Month]
  when 'Reg-NewFunded' then  [Reg-NewFunded Last Month Same Month]
  ```

- **Date (Month / Year)**

  ```
  (DATEPART('year', [Date])*100 + DATEPART('month', [Date]))
  ```

- **Demo-FTD**

  ```
  SUM([FTD])/
  SUM([FirstDemoTrade])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD % Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month]/[Demo-FTD Last 12 Months])-1
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 12 Months Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 12 months] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last 12 months] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 8 Weeks Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month]-[Demo-FTD Last 12 Months])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 12 Months Same Month**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month]-[Demo-FTD 12 Months Same Month])
  ```

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week]-[Demo-FTD 8 Weeks])
  ```

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week]-[Demo-FTD 8 Weeks Same Week])
  ```

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month]-[Demo-FTD Prev Month Same Month])
  ```

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week]-[Demo-FTD Prev Week Same Week])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last 12 Months**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 12 months] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last 12 months] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Month] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last Month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Month] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last Month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Week] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Month Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [prev month] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Week Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Prev Week] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Same Month**

  ```
  sum(IF [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/sum([FirstDemoTrade])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Same Week**

  ```
  sum(IF [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/sum([FirstDemoTrade])
  ```

  ```
  IF [Last Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END
  ```

- **FirstDemoTrade Prev Month**

  ```
  IF [prev month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END
  ```

- **FirstDemoTrade Prev Week**

  ```
  IF [Prev Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded % Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded Last month])/(SUM([FirstNewFunded 12 months])/12))-1
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded % Diff 8 Weeks**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded Last Week])/(SUM([FirstNewFunded 8 Weeks])/8))-1
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded % Prev Month**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded Last month])/(SUM([FirstNewFunded Prev Month])))-1
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded % Prev Week**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded Last Week])/(SUM([FirstNewFunded Prev Week])))-1
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded 12 months**

  ```
  IF [Last 12 months] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded 8 Weeks**

  ```
  IF [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded Last month**

  ```
  IF [Last Month] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded Last Week**

  ```
  IF [Last Week] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded Prev Month**

  ```
  IF [prev month] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FirstNewFunded Prev Week**

  ```
  IF [Prev Week] then [FirstNewFunded] END
  ```

- **FTD % Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  (SUM([FTD Last month])/(SUM([FTD 12 months])/12))-1
  ```

- **FTD % Diff 8 Weeks**

  ```
  (SUM([FTD Last Week])/(SUM([FTD 8 Weeks])/8))-1
  ```

- **FTD % Diff Prev Month**

  ```
  (SUM([FTD Last month])/(SUM([FTD Prev Month])))-1
  ```

- **FTD % Diff Prev Week**

  ```
  (SUM([FTD Last Week])/(SUM([FTD Prev Week])))-1
  ```

  ```
  sum(IF [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and  [FirstNewFunded]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/sum([FTD])
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction**

  ```
  SUM([FirstAction])/SUM([FTD])
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction % Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  ([FTD-FirstAction Last month]/[FTD-FirstAction Last 12 Months])-1
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction 12 Months Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 12 months] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  sum(if [Last 12 months] then [FTD] end)
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstAction] END)/
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FTD] end)
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction 8 Weeks Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 8 weeks] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FTD] end)
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction Diff 12 Months**

  ```
  ([FTD-FirstAction Last month]-[FTD-FirstAction Last 12 Months])
  ```

- **FTD-FirstAction Diff 12 Months Same Month**

  ```
  ([FTD-FirstAction Last Month Same Month]-[FTD-FirstAction 12 Months Same Month])

  ```

  ```

  ```

- **FTDA Tier**

  ```
  IF     [FTDA] < 50 AND [FTDA]>0 then '1-49'
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 100 then '50-99'
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 200 then '100-199' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 500 then '200-499' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 1000 then '500-999' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 5000 then '1,000-4,999' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] >= 5000 then '5,000+' 
  else '0'
  END
  ```

- **Key Markets**

  ```
  IF [New Marketing Region]='SEA'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Latam'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Australia'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Arabic'
      or [New Marketing Region]='ROW'
  then 'Non-EU'
  
  ELSEIF [New Marketing Region]='UK'
      or [New Marketing Region]='German'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Italian'
      or [New Marketing Region]='French'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Spain'
      or [New Marketing Region]='CEE'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Nordics'
      or [New Marketing Region]='ROE'
  then 'EU'
  
  ELSEIF [New Marketing Region]='USA' 
  then 'USA'  
  
  END
  ```

- **Last 12 months**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) >= dateadd('month',-14,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) <= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 2 months **

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) >= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) <= dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 2 Weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 20 weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-21,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 8 week Avg KPI**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 8 weeks] THEN [Chosen KPI] END)/8
  ```

- **Last 8 weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-9,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 8 weeks (include last week)**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-8,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last Month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last Month KPI**

  ```
  IF [Last Month] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

- **Last Week**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last week KPI**

  ```
  IF [Last Week] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

- **Lead score**

  ```
  IF  [Cluster] IN ('1','2','3') Then 'Low' 
  ELSEIF   [Cluster] IN ('4','5','6') THEN 'Medium'
  ELSEIF  [Cluster] IN ('7','8','9','10') THEN 'High'
  ELSE 'No cluster' 
  END
  ```

- **prev month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Prev Month KPI**

  ```
  IF [prev month] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Prev week KPI**

  ```
  IF [Prev Week] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

  ```
  ([Reg-V1 Last month]-[Reg-V1 Prev Month])
  ```

- **Reg-V1 Diff rev Week**

  ```
  ([Reg-V1 Last Week]-[Reg-V1 Prev Week])
  ```

- **Reg-V1 Last 12 Months**

  ```
  sum(if [Last 12 months] then [VerificationLevel1] END)/sum(if [Last 12 months] then [Registration] END)
  ```

- **Reg-V1 Last 12 Months Same Month**

  ```
  sum(if [Last 12 months] AND [Reg_this_MONTH]=1 and [VerificationLevel1]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  sum(if [Last 12 months] then [Registration] END)
  ```

- **Reg-V1 Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [VerificationLevel1] END)/sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [Registration] END)
  ```

- **Reg-V1 Last 8 Weeks Same Week**

  ```
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] AND [Reg_this_week]=1 and [VerificationLevel1]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [Registration] END)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Last Month] then [VerificationLevel1] END)/sum(if [Last Month] then [Registration] END)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [prev month] then [Registration] END)
  ```

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (BI_DB)

- **% Cross 14 days**

  ```
  sum([Cross14days]) / count([CID])
  ```

- **% Funded 14 days**

  ```
  sum([Funded14days]) / count([CID])
  ```

- **% Second Action 14 days**

  ```
  SUM([SecondAction14days])/ COUNT([CID])
  ```

- **choose KPI**

  ```
  CASE [choose KPI]
  WHEN 'First Time Funded' THEN COUNT([CID])
  WHEN 'Revenue 14 dayes' THEN AVG([Revenue14days])
  WHEN 'Deposit 14 days' THEN AVG([Deposit14days])
  WHEN 'AVG FTDA' THEN AVG([FirstDepositAmount])
  WHEN  '% Cross 14 days' THEN [% Cross 14 days] 
  WHEN '% Second Action 14 days' THEN [% Second Action 14 days] 
  END
  ```

- **Dynamic calculation**

  ```
  IF  [choose KPI] = 'First Time Funded' THEN WINDOW_AVG([choose KPI],-5,0)/5
  ELSEIF  [choose KPI] = 'AVG FTDA' THEN WINDOW_AVG([choose KPI],-5,0)
  ELSE NULL 
  END
  ```

- **KPI % change from avg 5 month**

  ```
  [choose KPI]/ WINDOW_AVG([choose KPI],-5,-1)-1
  ```

- **last 2 months**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[FirstNewFundedDate]) >= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[FirstNewFundedDate]) <= dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **last 5 months**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[FirstNewFundedDate]) >= dateadd('month',-6,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[FirstNewFundedDate]) <= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **last month **

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[FirstNewFundedDate]) = dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **split by**

  ```
  if [split by]='Region' then [NewMarketingRegion]
  ELSEIF [split by]='Channel' then [Channel]
  ELSEIF [split by]='Gender' then [Gender]
  ELSEIF  [split by] = 'First Action' then [FirstAction]
  ELSE '' END
  ```

### Workbook: Acquisition Weekly Dashboard

#### Datasource: CFO Dashboard-Data (local copy)

- **% change from last 5 months choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last Month KPI])/([Last 5 Months Avg KPI])-1
  ```

- **% change from last 8 weeks choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last week KPI])/([Last 8 week Avg KPI])-1
  ```

- **% change from Prev month choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last Month KPI])/SUM([Prev Month KPI])-1
  ```

- **% change from Prev week choose KPIs**

  ```
  SUM([Last week KPI])/SUM([Prev week KPI])-1
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Demo-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([Demo-FTD],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Demo-FTD],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: DeppAtt-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([DeppAtt-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([DeppAtt-FTD],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([DeppAtt-FTD],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: FirstCross-First Action-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([First Action-First Cross]-WINDOW_AVG([First Action-First Cross],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([First Action-First Cross],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: FirstDemoTrade-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstDemoTrade])-WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstDemoTrade]),-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstDemoTrade]),-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: FirstNewFunded-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (SUM([FirstNewFunded])-WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstNewFunded]),-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(SUM([FirstNewFunded]),-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: FTD-FirstAction-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([FTD-FirstAction]-WINDOW_AVG([FTD-FirstAction],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([FTD-FirstAction],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: FTDs-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([FTD])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([FTD]),-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([FTD]),-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Reg-Demo-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-Demo]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-Demo],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-Demo],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Reg-FTD-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-FTD]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-FTD],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-FTD],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Reg-NewFunded-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-New Funded]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-New Funded],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-New Funded],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Reg-V1-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Reg-V1]-WINDOW_AVG([Reg-V1],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Reg-V1],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: Regs-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([Registration])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([Registration]),-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([Registration]),-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: SecondAction-FirstAction-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([FirstAction-SecondAction]-WINDOW_AVG([FirstAction-SecondAction],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([FirstAction-SecondAction],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: V1-V2-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V1-V2]-WINDOW_AVG([V1-V2],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V1-V2],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Months: V2-V3-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V2-V3]-WINDOW_AVG([V2-V3],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V2-V3],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% Diff 5 Moths: V3-DeppAtt-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([V3-DeppAtt]-WINDOW_AVG([V3-DeppAtt],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([V3-DeppAtt],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG 8 Weeks-ABS-AVG WIN**

  ```
  (sum([Chosen KPI])-WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-8,-1))/WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-8,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG-ABS-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen KPI],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Chosen KPI],-5,-1)
  ```

- **% diff from AVG-CVR-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen CVR KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-5,-1))/WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-5,-1)
  ```

- **0**

  ```
  0
  ```

- **5 Months diff from AVG-CVR-AVG WIN**

  ```
  ([Chosen CVR KPI]-WINDOW_AVG([Chosen CVR KPI],-5,-1))
  ```

- **Chosen CVR KPI**

  ```
  case [Choose CVR KPI]
  when 'Reg-Demo' THEN [Reg-Demo]
  when 'Demo-FTD' then  [Demo-FTD]
  when 'Reg-V1' then  [Reg-V1]
  when 'V1-V2' then  [V1-V2]
  when 'V2-V3' then  [V2-V3]
  when 'V3-DeppAtt' then  [V3-DeppAtt]
  when 'DeppAtt-FTD' then  [DeppAtt-FTD]
  when 'Reg-FTD' then  [Reg-FTD]
  when 'Reg-NewFunded' then  [Reg-New Funded]
  when 'FTD-FirstAction' then  [FTD-FirstAction]
  when 'FirstAction-SecondAction' then  [FirstAction-SecondAction]
  when 'FirstAction-FirstCross' then  [First Action-First Cross]
  END
  ```

- **Chosen KPI**

  ```
  CASE   [Choose KPI]
  WHEN 'FTD' THEN [FTD]
  WHEN 'Registrations' then  [Registration]
  WHEN 'FirstDemoTrade' then  [FirstDemoTrade]
  WHEN 'FirstNewFunded' then  [FirstNewFunded]
  WHEN 'V1' then [VerificationLevel1]
  WHEN 'V2' then  [VerificationLevel2]
  WHEN 'V3' then  [VerificationLevel3]
  WHEN 'FirstAction' then  [FirstAction]
  WHEN 'SecondAction' then [SecondAction]
  WHEN 'FirstCross' then [FirstCross] 
  END
  ```

- **Chosen KPI-AVG 5 Months-AVG WIN**

  ```
  WINDOW_AVG(sum([Chosen KPI]),-5,-1)
  ```

- **Current month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = DATETRUNC('month',TODAY())
  ```

- **Current Week **

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = DATETRUNC('week',TODAY())
  ```

- **Date (Month / Year)**

  ```
  (DATEPART('year', [Date])*100 + DATEPART('month', [Date]))
  ```

- **date(day) **

  ```
  DATE(DATETRUNC('day',[Date] ))
  ```

- **date(month)**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date])
  ```

- **date(week)**

  ```
  DATE(DATETRUNC('week',[Date]))
  ```

- **Demo-FTD**

  ```
  SUM([FTD])/
  SUM([FirstDemoTrade])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD % Diff 5 Months**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month]/[Demo-FTD Last 5 Months])-1
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 5 Months Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 5 months] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last 5 months] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD 8 Weeks Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last 8 weeks] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 5 Months**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month]-[Demo-FTD Last 5 Months])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 5 Months Same Month**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month]-[Demo-FTD 5 Months Same Month])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 8 Weeks**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week]-[Demo-FTD 8 Weeks])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff 8 Weeks Same Week**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week]-[Demo-FTD 8 Weeks Same Week])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff Prev Month**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month]-[Demo-FTD Prev Month])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff Prev Month Same Month**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month]-[Demo-FTD Prev Month Same Month])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff Prev Week**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week]-[Demo-FTD Prev Week])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Diff Prev Week Same Week**

  ```
  ([Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week]-[Demo-FTD Prev Week Same Week])
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last 5 Months**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last 5 months] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last 5 months] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [last month] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [last month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Month Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [last month] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [last month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Last Week Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Last Week] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Last Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Month Same Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [prev month] and [FTD_this_MONTH]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [prev month] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FTD] END)/
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```

- **Demo-FTD Prev Week Same Week**

  ```
  SUM(if [Prev Week] and [FTD_this_week]=1 and [FirstDemoTrade]=1 then 1 else 0 END)/
  SUM(if [Prev Week] then [FirstDemoTrade] END)
  ```


- **FTDA Tier**

  ```
  IF     [FTDA] < 100 AND [FTDA]>0 then '1-99'
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 200 then '100-199' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 500 then '200-499' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 1000 then '500-999' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] < 5000 then '1,000-4,999' 
  ELSEIF [FTDA] >= 5000 then '5,000+' 
  else '0'
  END
  ```

- **Key Markets**

  ```
  IF [New Marketing Region]='SEA'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Latam'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Australia'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Arabic'
      or [New Marketing Region]='ROW'
  then 'Non-EU'
  
  ELSEIF [New Marketing Region]='UK'
      or [New Marketing Region]='German'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Italian'
      or [New Marketing Region]='French'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Spain'
      or [New Marketing Region]='CEE'
      or [New Marketing Region]='Nordics'
      or [New Marketing Region]='ROE'
  then 'EU'
  
  ELSEIF [New Marketing Region]='USA' 
  then 'USA'  
  
  END
  ```

- **Last 2 months **

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) >= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) <= dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 2 Weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 20 weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-21,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 5 months**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) >= dateadd('month',-6,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) <= dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 5 Months Avg KPI**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 5 months] THEN [Chosen KPI] END)/5
  ```

- **Last 8 week Avg KPI**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Last 8 weeks] THEN [Chosen KPI] END)/8
  ```

- **Last 8 weeks**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-9,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last 8 weeks (include last week)**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) >= dateadd('week',-8,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  and DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) <= dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **last month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = dateadd('month',-1,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last Month KPI**

  ```
  IF [last month] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

- **Last Week**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = dateadd('week',-1,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Last week KPI**

  ```
  IF [Last Week] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

- **Lead score**

  ```
  IF  [Cluster] IN ('1','2','3') Then 'Low' 
  ELSEIF   [Cluster] IN ('4','5','6') THEN 'Medium'
  ELSEIF  [Cluster] IN ('7','8','9','10') THEN 'High'
  ELSE 'No cluster' 
  END
  ```

- **prev month**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date]) = dateadd('month',-2,DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Prev Month KPI**

  ```
  IF [prev month] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

- **Prev Week**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('week',[Date]) = dateadd('week',-2,DATETRUNC('week',TODAY()))
  ```

- **Prev week KPI**

  ```
  IF [Prev Week] THEN [Chosen KPI] END
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] AND [V1_this_week]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/
  sum(if [Last 8 weeks] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Last month**

  ```
  sum(if [last month] then [VerificationLevel2] END)/sum(if [last month] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Last Month Same Month**

  ```
  sum(if [last month] AND [V1_this_MONTH]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/
  sum(if [last month] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Last Week**

  ```
  sum(if [Last Week] then [VerificationLevel2] END)/sum(if [Last Week] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Last Week Same Week**

  ```
  sum(if [Last Week] AND [V1_this_week]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/
  sum(if [Last Week] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Prev Month**

  ```
  sum(if [prev month] then [VerificationLevel2] END)/
  sum(if [prev month] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Prev Month Same Month**

  ```
  sum(if [prev month] AND [V1_this_MONTH]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/
  sum(if [prev month] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Prev Week] then [VerificationLevel2] END)/sum(if [Prev Week] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

- **V1-V2 Prev Week Same Week**

  ```
  sum(if [Prev Week] AND [V1_this_week]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/
  sum(if [Prev Week] then [VerificationLevel1] END)
  ```

  ```

  ```

- **V1-V2 Same Week**

  ```
  sum(if [V1_this_week]=1 and [VerificationLevel2]=1 then 1 else 0 end)/sum([VerificationLevel1])
  ```

  ```

  ```

  ```
  if [VerificationLevelID]=3 then [VerificationLevel3Date]

  end
  ```

### Workbook: Club Upgrade Visibility

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **Amount To Upgrade**

  ```
  IF [CurrentTier] = 1 THEN 5000- [ClubEquity] 
  ELSEIF [CurrentTier] = 5 THEN 10000 - [ClubEquity]
  ELSEIF [CurrentTier] = 3 THEN 25000 - [ClubEquity]
  ELSEIF [CurrentTier] = 2 THEN 50000 - [ClubEquity]
  ELSEIF [CurrentTier] = 6 THEN 250000 - [ClubEquity]
  ELSE 0 END
  ```


### Workbook: Daily Product KPI Dashboard

#### Datasource: acquisition

- **% change first action**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [First_action] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change first action>funded**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [Funded] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [Funded] ELSE NULL end)/
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change ftd**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [FTDs] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change ftd>first action**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end)/
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change funded**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [Funded] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [Funded] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change reg**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [Reg] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change reg>v1**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end)/
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v1**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [V1]
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change v1>v2**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end)/
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v2**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [V2] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change v2>v3**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end)/
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v3**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [Date]!=[Yesterday]
      THEN [V3] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **% change v3>ftd**

  ```
  (SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF[Date]= [Yesterday] THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[Date]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) and [Date]!=[Yesterday] THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end)/
  ```
