- **Avg. last 8 weeks**

  ```
  IF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=1 then 'Sunday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=2 then 'Monday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=3 then 'Tuesday' 
  ELSEIF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=4 then 'Wednesday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=5 then 'Thursday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=6 then 'Friday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=7 then 'Saturday' 
  ELSE NULL end
  ```

- **CVR First Action > Funded**

  ```
  sum([Funded])/sum([First_action])
  ```

- **CVR FTD > First Action**

  ```
  sum([First_action])/sum([FTDs])
  ```

- **CVR Reg>V1**

  ```
  sum([V1])/sum([Reg])
  ```

- **CVR V1>V2**

  ```
  sum([V2])/sum([V1])
  ```

- **CVR V2>V3**

  ```
  sum([V3])/sum([V2])
  ```

- **CVR V3 > FTD**

  ```
  sum([FTDs])/sum([V3])
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  TODAY()-1
  ```

#### Datasource: acquisition (2)

- **% change first action**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [First_action] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change first action>funded**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [Funded] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [Funded] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change ftd**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [FTDs] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change ftd>first action**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [First_action] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [First_action] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change funded**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [Funded] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Funded] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change reg**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Reg] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change reg>v1**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V1] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [Reg] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v1**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V1] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change v1>v2**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V2] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V1] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v2**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V2] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change v2>v3**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V3] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V2] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V2]  ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **% change v3**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V3] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **% change v3>ftd**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [FTDs] END)/SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null' THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end))
  /
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [FTDs] ELSE NULL end)/SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE THEN [V3] ELSE NULL end))
  -1
  ```

- **avg cvr first action>funded last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Funded] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [First_action] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)
  ```

- **avg cvr ftd>first action last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [First_action] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [FTDs] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)
  ```

- **avg cvr reg>v1 last 5 months**

  ```
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V1] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)/
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Reg] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)
  ```

- **avg cvr v1>v2 last 5 months**

  ```
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V2] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)
  /
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V1] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)
  ```

- **avg cvr v2>v3 last 5 months**

  ```
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V3] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)/
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V2] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)
  ```

- **avg cvr v3>ftd last 5 months**

  ```
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [FTDs] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)/
  (SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V3] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)
  ```

- **avg first action last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [First_action] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg ftd last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [FTDs] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg funded last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Funded] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg reg last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [Reg] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg v1 last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V1] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg v2 last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V2] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **avg v3 last 5 months**

  ```
  SUM(IF isnull([LastMonth])=TRUE
      THEN [V3] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5
  ```

- **Avg. last 8 weeks**

  ```
  IF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=1 then 'Sunday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=2 then 'Monday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=3 then 'Tuesday' 
  ELSEIF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=4 then 'Wednesday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=5 then 'Thursday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=6 then 'Friday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=7 then 'Saturday' 
  ELSE NULL end
  ```

- **CVR First Action > Funded**

  ```
  sum([Funded])/sum([First_action])
  ```

- **CVR FTD > First Action**

  ```
  sum([First_action])/sum([FTDs])
  ```

- **CVR Reg>V1**

  ```
  sum([V1])/sum([Reg])
  ```

- **CVR V1>V2**

  ```
  sum([V2])/sum([V1])
  ```

- **CVR V2>V3**

  ```
  sum([V3])/sum([V2])
  ```

- **CVR V3 > FTD**

  ```
  sum([FTDs])/sum([V3])
  ```

- **LastMonth**

  ```
  IF YEAR([Date])=YEAR(DATEADD('month',-1,TODAY())) AND MONTH([Date])=MONTH(DATEADD('month',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN LEFT(STR([Date]),4)+RIGHT(LEFT(STR([Date]),7),2) END
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  TODAY()-1
  ```

#### Datasource: MIMO Synapse

- **% Change Cashout**

  ```
  ([Cashout Users]/[Avg Cashout Same Days Last 8 Weeks])-1
  ```

- **% Change Deposit**

  ```
  ([Deposit Users]/[Avg Deposit Users Same Day 8 Weeks])-1
  ```

- **% Change FTD**

  ```
  ([FTD Users]/[Avg FTD Users Same 8 Weeks])-1
  ```

- **% Change NMI**

  ```
  ([Net Money In Users]/[Avg Net Money In Users Same 8 Weeks])-1
  ```

- **% Change Redeposit**

  ```
  ([ReDeposit Users]/[Avg Redeposit Users Same Days 8 Weeks])-1
  ```

- **Avg Cashout Same Days Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN [IsCashedOut] END)/COUNTD( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN DATE([Date])END )
  ```

- **Avg Deposit Users Same Day 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN [IsDeposit] END)/COUNTD( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN DATE([Date])END )
  ```

- **Avg FTD Users Same 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN [IsFirstDeposit] END)/COUNTD( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN DATE([Date])END )
  ```

- **Avg Net Money In Users Same 8 Weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN [NMI_User] END )/COUNTD( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN DATE([Date])END )
  ```

- **Avg Redeposit Users Same Days 8 Weeks**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [IsReDeposit] >0 and [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN [CID] END)/COUNTD( IF [IsYesterday] = FALSE THEN DATE([Date])END )
  ```

- **Cashout Actions**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [CashoutsCount] END)
  ```

- **Cashout Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [CashoutsAmount] END)
  ```

- **Cashout Users**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [IsCashedOut] END)
  ```

- **Cashout Users Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub] AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsCashedOut] END)
  ```

- **Cashout Users Non Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub]=FALSE  AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsCashedOut] END)
  ```

- **Date**

  ```
  DATEADD('day',-1,[EOD])
  ```

- **Deposit Actions**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [DepositsCount] END)
  ```

- **Deposit Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [DepositsAmount] END)
  ```

- **Deposit Users**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [IsDeposit] END)
  ```

- **Depositors Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub] AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsDeposit] END )
  ```

- **Depositors Non Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub]=FALSE  AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsDeposit] END )
  ```

- **FTD Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [FirstDepositAmounts] END)
  ```

- **FTD Users**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [IsFirstDeposit] END)
  ```

- **FTDs Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub] AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsFirstDeposit] END)
  ```

- **FTDs Non Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub]=FALSE  AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsFirstDeposit] END)
  ```

- **IsClub**

  ```
  [PlayerLevel (group)] = 'Club'
  ```

- **IsRedeposit Actions**

  ```
  [Deposit Actions] - [FTD Users]
  ```

- **IsRedeposit Amount**

  ```
  [Deposit Amount] - [FTD Amount]
  ```

- **IsRedeposit Club**

  ```
  //COUNTD(IF [IsClub] AND [IsReDeposit] >0 THEN [CID] END)
  SUM(IF [IsClub] AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsReDeposit] END)
  ```

- **IsRedeposit Non Club**

  ```
  //COUNTD(IF [IsClub] AND [IsReDeposit] >0 THEN [CID] END)
  SUM(IF [IsClub]=FALSE  AND [IsYesterday] THEN [IsReDeposit] END)
  ```

- **IsYesterday**

  ```
  DATEADD('day',-1,[EOD])= DATE(TODAY()-1)
  ```

- **Net Money In Actions**

  ```
  [Deposit Actions] + [Cashout Actions]
  ```

- **Net Money In Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [NetMoneyIn] END)
  ```

- **Net Money In Users**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsYesterday] THEN [NMI_User] END)
  ```

- **NMI Club**

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub] AND [IsYesterday] THEN [NMI_User] END)
  ```

- **NMI Non Club **

  ```
  SUM(IF [IsClub]=FALSE AND [IsYesterday] THEN [NMI_User] END)
  ```

- **ReDeposit Users**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [IsReDeposit] >0 AND [IsYesterday] THEN [CID] END)
  ```

#### Datasource: NPS

- **NPS Score**

  ```
  100* (if [Score] = 9 or [Score] = 10 then 1
      elseif [Score] >=0 and [Score] < 7 then -1
          elseif [Score] = 7 or [Score] = 8 then 0
          END)
  ```

- **NPS Score Club**

  ```
  IF [Club Tier (group)] = 'Club'  THEN 100* (if [Score] = 9 or [Score] = 10 then 1
      elseif [Score] >=0 and [Score] < 7 then -1
          elseif [Score] = 7 or [Score] = 8 then 0
          END) END
  ```

- **NPS Score Non-Club**

  ```
  IF [Club Tier (group)] = 'Non-Club'  THEN 100* (if [Score] = 9 or [Score] = 10 then 1
      elseif [Score] >=0 and [Score] < 7 then -1
          elseif [Score] = 7 or [Score] = 8 then 0
          END) END
  ```

#### Datasource: Retention Synapse

- **% Active Traders From Total**

  ```
  [Active Traders]/[Active Users]
  ```

- **%Active Copiers From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Active Smart Portfolios Investors From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%CFD Traders From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%change Active Users**

  ```
  ([Active Users]/[avg Active Users last 8 weeks])-1
  ```

- **%change Amount**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])) THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])) THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount CFD**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount copy**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]!=4 
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]!=4
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount copy portfolio**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' 
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' THEN [Amount]
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount crypto**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount equities**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount investors**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1)OR [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [Amount] ELSE NULL end))/
  (SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1)OR  [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change AO**

  ```
  (COUNTD(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]) THEN [concat CID+ week num] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNTD(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]) THEN [concat CID+ week num] ELSE NULL end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change CFD**

  ```
  (COUNTD(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [concat CID+ week num] ELSE NULL end))/

      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [concat CID+ week num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change copy**

  ```

      AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [MirrorTypeId_null]!=4 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  ```

- **%change New Trades**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])) THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])) THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades CFD**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/

      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [PositionID]

  ```

- **%change New Trades copy**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]!=4// AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]!=4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades copy portfolio**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades crypto**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades equities**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades investors**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [OpenDate]= [Yesterday] AND (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1)OR [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
   THEN [PositionID] ELSE NULL end))/
  (COUNT(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      AND [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1)OR  [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8)-1
  ```

- **%Crypto Traders From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Equities Traders From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **0**

  ```
  0
  ```

- **0 (copy)**

  ```
  ''
  ```

- **Active Copiers**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] THEN [CID] END)
  //COUNTD(IF [MirrorTypeID] = '1' THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **Active Smart Portfolios Investors**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **Active Traders**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]=0 OR [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **Active Users**

  ```
  COUNT(IF [Date] = [Yesterday] THEN [GCID (Custom SQL Query1)] END)
  ```

- **avg Active Users last 8 weeks**

  ```
  COUNT([GCID (Custom SQL Query1)])/8
  ```

- **avg Amount CFD last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0))
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount copy last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
         AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount copy portfolio last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
         AND [MirrorTypeID]='4'// AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount crypto last 8 weeks **

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount equities last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) 
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount investors last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) 
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg Amount last 8 weeks**

  ```
  SUM(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND  ([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]))
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg AO last 8 weeks**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
      and [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])
      THEN [concat CID+ week num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg CFD last 8 weeks**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0))
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [concat CID+ week num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg copy last 8 weeks**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND [MirrorID]<>0
         AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [concat CID+ week num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg copy portfolio last 8 weeks**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF DATEPART('weekday',[OpenDate]) = DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday]) 
         AND  [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
         AND [MirrorID]<>0
         AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [concat CID+ week num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **avg New Trades last 8 weeks**

  ```

      and [OpenDate]!=[Yesterday]
      AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]))
      THEN [PositionID] 
      //ELSE NULL 
  end)/8
  ```

- **Avg. Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  IF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=1 then 'Sunday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=2 then 'Monday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=3 then 'Tuesday' 
  ELSEIF DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=4 then 'Wednesday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=5 then 'Thursday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=6 then 'Friday' 
  ELSEIF  DATEPART('weekday',[Yesterday])=7 then 'Saturday' 
  ELSE NULL end
  ```

- **CFD Traders**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **concat CID+ week num**

  ```
  str([CID])+str([week number])
  ```

- **Copy & Portfolios Amount - Copy**

  ```
  SUM(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Copy & Portfolios Amount - Smart Portfolio**

  ```
  SUM(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Copy & Portfolios New Trades - Copy**

  ```
  COUNT(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **Copy & Portfolios New Trades - Smart Portfolio**

  ```
  COUNT(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] 
  THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **Crypto Traders**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **Equities Traders**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **Invest Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF [MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]) THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Investing Amount - Crypto**

  ```
  SUM(IF [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Investing Amount - Equities**

  ```
  SUM(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Investing New Trades - Crypto**

  ```
  COUNT(IF [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **Investing New Trades - Equities**

  ```
  COUNT(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **Investord Real Assets Amount**

  ```
  SUM(IF (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) OR [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Investord Real Assets New Trades**

  ```
  COUNT(IF (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) OR [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **Investord Real Assets Users **

  ```
  COUNTD(IF (([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) OR [InstrumentType]='Crypto Currencies') AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)
  ```

- **IsClub Blended **

  ```
  [PlayerLevelID (Custom SQL Query1)] in (2,3,5,6,7)
  or [PlayerLevelID] in (2,3,5,6,7)
  ```

- **IsNonClub Blended**

  ```
  [PlayerLevelID (Custom SQL Query1)] = 1
  or [PlayerLevelID] = 1
  ```

- **IsYesterday Blended**

  ```
  [Date] = [Yesterday]
  or [OpenDate] = [Yesterday]
  ```

- **Leveraged Amont - CFD**

  ```
  SUM(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [Amount] END)
  ```

- **Leveraged New Trades - CFD**

  ```
  COUNT(IF ([InstrumentType] IN ('Indices','Currencies','Commodities') 
        OR ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) )
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **MirrorTypeId_null**

  ```
  CASE [MirrorTypeID] WHEN '4' THEN 4 ELSE 1 END
  ```

- **New Trades**

  ```
  COUNT(IF [MirrorID]=0 OR  ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror])  //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

- **week number**

  ```
  WEEK([OpenDate])
  ```

- **weekend**

  ```
  ISOWEEKDAY([OpenDate])
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  TODAY()-1
  ```

#### Datasource: Retention Synapse (2)

- **% Active Traders From Total**

  ```
  [Active Traders]/[Active Users]
  ```

- **%Active Copiers From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth] THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Active Smart Portfolios Investors From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [MirrorID]>0 AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth] THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%CFD Stocks From Tota**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%change Active Users**

  ```
  ((COUNTD(IF [LastMonth]=[OpenYearMonth] AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth]) THEN [CID] END))/
  [avg AO last 5 Months])-1
  ```

- **%change Amount**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
      AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth])) THEN [Amount] END))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      AND  (([MirrorID]=0 OR ([MirrorID]>0) AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth]))
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount CFD Stocks**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [Amount] END))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0)
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change Amount Commodities**

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
      AND [InstrumentType]='Commodities'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [Amount] END))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      AND [InstrumentType]='Commodities'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [Amount] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

  ```
  (SUM(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
      AND [MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 THEN [Amount] END))/
  (SUM(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [MirrorID]<>0 AND  [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth]
         AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [Amount] 
  ```
  ```
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change Indices**

  ```
  (COUNTD(IF [LastMonth]=[OpenYearMonth] AND [InstrumentType] ='Indices'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END))/
  (COUNTD(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [InstrumentType]='Indices'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [concat CID+ YearMonth num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
         AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth]))  //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
      AND ([MirrorID]=0 OR  ([MirrorID]>0 AND  [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth]))
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades CFD Stocks**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])!=TRUE 
         AND  ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=0)
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades Commodities**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
        AND [InstrumentType]='Commodities'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [InstrumentType]='Commodities'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades copy**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])!=TRUE
          and [MirrorID]>0 AND  [LastMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth] AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
   THEN [PositionID] END))/
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND ([MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth])
         AND [MirrorTypeId_null]<>4 //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades copy portfolio**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])!=TRUE
         AND [MirrorID]>0 AND [LastMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth] AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror] 
  THEN [PositionID] END))/
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND ([MirrorID]>0 AND [OpenYearMonth]=[OpenMirrorYearMonth])
         AND [MirrorTypeID]='4' //AND [OpenDate]=[OpenMirror]
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades crypto**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
         AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades Currencies**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
        AND [InstrumentType]='Currencies'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [InstrumentType]='Currencies'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades Indices**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF [LastMonth]!='Null'
        AND [InstrumentType]='Indices'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND [InstrumentType]='Indices'
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change New Trades Real Stocks**

  ```
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])!=TRUE 
         AND  ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [PositionID] END))
  /
  (COUNT(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1)
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [PositionID] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%change Real Stocks**

  ```
  (COUNTD(IF [LastMonth]=[OpenYearMonth] AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END))/
  (COUNTD(IF ISNULL([LastMonth])=TRUE
         AND ([InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1) 
         AND [MirrorID]=0 
  
      THEN [concat CID+ YearMonth num] 
      ELSE NULL 
  end)/5)-1
  ```

- **%Commodities From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType]='Commodities'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Crypto From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType] ='Crypto Currencies' AND [MirrorID]=0
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Currencies From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType]='Currencies'
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Indices From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType]='Indices' 
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

- **%Real Stocks From Total**

  ```
  COUNTD(IF [InstrumentType] IN ('ETF','Stocks') AND [IsSettled]=1
        AND [MirrorID]=0      
  THEN [CID] END)/[Active Traders]
  ```

  ```

  ```


- **IsClub Blended **

  ```
  [PlayerLevelID] in (2,3,5,6,7)
  ```

- **IsLastMonth Blended**

  ```
  [OpenYearMonth] = [LastMonth]
  ```

- **IsNonClub Blended**

  ```
  [PlayerLevelID] = 1
  ```

- **LastMonth**

  ```
  IF YEAR([OpenDate])=YEAR(DATEADD('month',-1,TODAY())) AND MONTH([OpenDate])=MONTH(DATEADD('month',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN LEFT(STR([OpenDate]),4)+RIGHT(LEFT(STR([OpenDate]),7),2) END
  ```

- **MirrorTypeId_null**

  ```
  CASE [MirrorTypeID] WHEN '4' THEN 4 ELSE 1 END
  ```

  ```
   THEN [PositionID] END)
  ```

### Workbook: Delta App Dashboard

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **Calculation2**

  ```
  [EOMRegisteredReal]
  ```

- **Funded**

  ```
  IF  [EOMFirstNewFundedDate] = [Date] THEN [RealCID] ELSE NULL END
  ```

- **Funded (copy)**

  ```
  IF  MONTH([EOMFirstNewFundedDate]) =  MONTH([RegisteredReal]) THEN [RealCID] ELSE NULL END
  ```

- **MaxDate**

  ```
  {fixed :max([EOMRegisteredReal]) }
  ```

- **Registered this month**

  ```
  IF   [EOMRegisteredReal] = [Date] THEN [RealCID] ELSE NULL END
  ```

- **Total Running Funded**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(COUNTD([Funded (copy)]))
  ```

- **Total Running Reg **

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(COUNT([RealCID]))
  ```

- **Total Running Upgrade**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(COUNTD([Total Upgrade to date]))
  ```

- **Total Upgrade to date**

  ```
  IF [WasInClub] = 1 THEN [RealCID] ELSE NULL end
  ```

- **Upgrade**

  ```
  IF [EOMClubChangeLog]  = [Date] AND  [CurrentClub] <> 'Bronze' THEN [RealCID] ELSE NULL END
  ```

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (sql_dp_prod_we) (2)

- **Date parameter**

  ```
  [Date] = [Date] or MONTH([Date]) = MONTH([Date])
  ```

### Workbook: IR Dashboard

#### Datasource: AUA

- **AUA O.B**

  ```
  LOOKUP(SUM([Amount]), -1)
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Date Filter For Cycle**

  ```
  RANK_UNIQUE(MAX([Date]), 'desc') <= [Months to Display]
  ```

- **info**

  ```
  max(1)
  ```

- **LoadDate AUA**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

- **PnL**

  ```
  SUM([Amount]) 
  - LOOKUP(SUM([Amount]), -1)
  - SUM([federated.1ifznqu042lok517q8dp405bhxhu].[Deposits])
  + SUM([federated.1ifznqu042lok517q8dp405bhxhu].[Calculation_1800313983448879119])
  ```

#### Datasource: Avg Staking

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **info**

  ```
  max(1)
  ```

- **Staking LoadDate**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

#### Datasource: Client funds

- **Avg Cash**

  ```
  sum([Total Cash])/max([Num_of_days])
  ```

- **Avg CFD (w/o FSA & FSRA)**

  ```
  sum([CFD Equity])/max([Num_of_days])
  ```

- **CFD Equity**

  ```
  if [Regulation] in ('FSA Seychelles','FSRA') THEN 0 ELSE  [Equity CFD] end
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Load Date Client funds**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 
  or dATEDIFF('day', MAX(([federated.0noh3780xdqner15ynnod11h8snh].[LoadDate])), TODAY()) > 0
  or dATEDIFF('day', MAX(([federated.1behsvt1wcebwa172y52s1snnzf7].[LoadDate])), TODAY()) > 0
  
  
  
  THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

- **Total Interest Client Balance**

  ```
  ZN([Avg CFD (w/o FSA & FSRA)])+ZN([Avg Cash])+SUM(ZN([federated.1behsvt1wcebwa172y52s1snnzf7].[AvgOpenPosition]))+SUM(ZN([federated.1hw9a300zmwbgk1bxwbtg1qngkdv].[Avg_eMoney_BalanceUSD]))+SUM(ZN([federated.0noh3780xdqner15ynnod11h8snh].[Avg_Value_OptIn]))
  ```

### Workbook: Onboarding Operations Excellence Report

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (BI_DB)

- **Experienced Ind**

  ```
  IF[Experience_Level (group)]='Experienced' then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **sum([Q3_Is_Professional_Knowledge])/count([RealCID])**

  ```
  sum([Q3_Is_Professional_Knowledge])/count([RealCID])
  ```

#### Datasource: Operations Onboarding KPIs

- **% of VL3 < 1Hr**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **% of VL3 < 24Hr**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 24
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **% of VL3 > 3Day**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) >= 72
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **%FA**

  ```
  [SUM FA]/[SUM Reg]
  ```

- **%STP POA**

  ```
  sum(if [POA IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POA_Manager]=0 or [POA_Manager]=Null) then 1 else 0 end)/count([CID])
  ```

- **%STP POI**

  ```
  sum(if[POI IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POI_Manager]=0 or [POI_Manager]=NULL) then 1 else 0 end )/count([CID])
  ```

- **%STP US**

  ```
  sum([Screening IsAutomatic])/count([CID])
  ```

- **calc: #Funded**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([calc: Funded]/5) else [calc: Funded] end)
  ```

- **calc: Dep.Attempt**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([DepositAttempt]/5) else [DepositAttempt] end)
  ```

- **calc: Funded**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **calc:#FA**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([FirstAction]/5) else [FirstAction] end)
  ```

- **calc:#Reg**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL0]/5) else [IsVL0] end)
  ```

- **calc:#VL1**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL1]/5) else [IsVL1] end)
  ```

- **calc:#VL2**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL2]/5) else [IsVL2] end)
  ```

- **calc:#VL3**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL3]/5) else [IsVL3] end)
  ```

- **calc:%Funded**

  ```
  sum([calc: Funded])/[SUM Reg]
  ```

- **calc:FTDs**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([Is FTD]/5) else [Is FTD] end)
  ```

  ```
  COUNT([CID]) / TOTAL(COUNT([CID]))
  ```


- **CID (copy)**

  ```
  [CID]
  ```

- **Closed Accounts**

  ```
  if [PlayerStatusID]=2 and [PlayerStatusReasonID]= 40 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Country average LTV**

  ```
  { FIXED [Country],month([DateTime VL2]):sum([LTV])/sum(if [LTV]>0 then 1 else 0 end)}
  ```

- **Country Heat Value**

  ```
  [Country]+' : '+ [Non Verification Sub reason]
  ```

- **Date of Registration**

  ```

  ```

- **DaysFrom FTD**

  ```

  ```

- **DD Hours RegtoVL3**

  ```
  [DDMinutes VL0toVL3] / 60
  ```

  ```
  ZN(COUNT([CID (copy)])) - LOOKUP(ZN(COUNT([CID (copy)])), -1)/ COUNT([CID (copy)])
  ```

- **Docs Flow**

  ```
  IF [VD HasDocuments] = 0 THEN "No Docs"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 1 AND [POA IsApproved] = 1 THEN "Both Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 1 AND [POA IsApproved] = 0 THEN "POI Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 0 AND [POA IsApproved] = 1 THEN "POA Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 0 AND [POA IsApproved] = 0 THEN "Both Declined"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **Document SLA**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=2 then 'In 0-2 Minutes'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=10 then'In 3-10 minutes'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=180 then'11 min - 3 hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=360 then '4-6 Hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=720 then '7-12 Hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=1440 then '13-24 Hours'
  ELSE 'More then 24 Hours'
  end
  ```

- **Effected VL2 customers**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL2])
  ```

- **EV Flow**

  ```
  IF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND ISNULL([EV MatchStatusID]) THEN "EV: Not Sent"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND [EV MatchStatusID] IN (1, 2) THEN "EV: Verified"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND [EV MatchStatusID] IN (0, 3) THEN "EV: Not Verified"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 0 THEN "Non-EV"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **EV MatchStatus (copy)**

  ```
  [EV MatchStatus]
  ```

- **EV verified #**

  ```
  sum (if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]='Verified' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **EV verified or other verification**

  ```
  if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]='Verified' then 'EV'
   
   else 'Not sent to EV' end
  ```

- **EV vs. NonEv Category**

  ```
  IF IFNULL([EV MatchStatusID], 0) = 0 THEN "Not sent to EV"
  ELSEIF [EV MatchStatusID] IN (1, 2, 3) THEN "Sent to EV"
  END
  ```

- **FA in Reg Month (copy)**

  ```
  if  MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([FirstActionDate])   then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **FA&FTD in Reg Month (copy)**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime FTD])
  and MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([FirstActionDate])   then 1 else 0 end
  ```

  ```
  if  month([Date of Registration])=month([FirstDepositAttemptDate])then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **FirstAction Ind**

  ```
  [FirstAction]
  ```

- **FTD before V3 Ind**

  ```
  if [DateTime FTD]<[DateTime VL3] then 'FTD Before V3'
  ELSEIF [DateTime FTD]>[DateTime VL3] then 'FTD After V3' 
  end
  ```

- **FTD EV Group**

  ```
  if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]<>'Verified' then 'Not Approved'
  elseif [FirstAction Ind]=1 then 'EV Approved+FA'
  elseif [FirstAction Ind]=0 then 'EV Approved+No FA'
  else 'Not Relevant' end
  ```

- **FTD in Reg Month**

  ```
  if  month([Date of Registration])=month([DateTime FTD]) 
  and year([Date of Registration])= year([DateTime FTD]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded and not Funded drill**

  ```
  IF [Funded FTD month]=1 then 'Funded - V3+FA'
  elseif [IsVL3]=1 then 'V3 No F.Action'
  ELSE 'No V3'
  end
  ```

- **Funded FTD month**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([FirstActionDate]) 
   and MONTH([DateTime FTD])>=MONTH([DateTime VL3])
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded FTD month (copy)**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([FirstActionDate]) 
   and MONTH([DateTime FTD])>=MONTH([DateTime VL3])
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([FirstActionDate])   then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Heat Map Value (AVG LTV*CIDs)**

- **IsVL3 (copy)**


- **Max Document Reviewed Date**


- **Max Document Upload Date**


- **Non Verification Sub reason**

  ```
  if
  [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=0 and [POI IsApproved]=0 then 'Both Docs Not Approved'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=1 and [POI IsApproved]=0 then 'POI Not Approved'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=0 and [POI IsApproved]=1 then 'POA Not Approved'
  
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=0 and zn([POI IsApproved])=0 then 'Missing Both Docs'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=1 and zn([POI IsApproved])=0 then 'Missing POI'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=0 and zn([POI IsApproved])=1 then 'Missing POA'
  
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='User Screening Issue' and ((ZN([POA IsApproved])=1 and zn([POI IsApproved])=1) or [EV MatchStatus]='Verified') and
  ([Phone Verification] ='AutomaticallyVerified' or [Phone Verification] ='ManualyVerified') then 'User Screening issue only'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='User Screening Issue' then 'User Screening with other issues'
  
  else [NonVerificationReason]
  end
  ```

- **Not Funded Group (FTD Month)**

  ```
  IF [Funded FTD month]=0 and [IsVL3]=0 then 'No V3'
  elseif [Funded FTD month]=0 and [IsVL3]=1 and [DateTime VL3]<= [DateTime FTD] then 'V3 Before FTD + No FA'
  else 'V3 After FTD + No FA'
  end
  ```

- **Period Ind**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind (copy)**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 1.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind _Week**

  ```
  if [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) then 'Curr
   Week'
  elseif [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-14,TODAY()) then 'Prev
  Week'
    elseif [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-70,TODAY()) then '8 Weeks
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind VL2**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind_Summary**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **POA Decline Category**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([POA CountDeclines]) THEN "No Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] = 1 THEN "One Decline"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] IN (2, 3) THEN "2 to 3 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] IN (4, 5) THEN "4 to 5 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] > 5 THEN "More than 5 Declines"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **POI Decline Category**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([POI CountDeclines]) THEN "No Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] = 1 THEN "One Decline"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] IN (2, 3) THEN "2 to 3 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] IN (4, 5) THEN "4 to 5 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] > 5 THEN "More than 5 Declines"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **POI/POA STP User %**

  ```
  if [IsVL3] = 1
             and ([EV MatchStatus]='None' or isnull([EV MatchStatus])=TRUE 
                  )
             and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'     
             and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
             and [DateTime VL2]>DATE("2022-08-14")
  and [POA IsApproved]+[POI IsApproved]=2 and [POA_Manager]+[POI_Manager]=0
   
      then 1 
  end
  ```

- **Regular STP User %**

  ```
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
           and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
           and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'
           and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
           and [Country ID]=219 
           and [Email Verification]=1
           THEN 1
       ELSEIF  [IsVL3] = 1 
               and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
               and ifnull([Screening Status],'NoMatch')='NoMatch'
               and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
               and [Designated Regulation]='CYSEC'
               and [Country ID]!=219 
               then 1 
      elseif [IsVL3] = 1
             and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
             and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'     
             and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
             and [Country ID]!=219
      then 1  
  
       else 0 END
  ```

- **STP 5 month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then zn([Regular STP User %])+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **STP 5 month diff abs (copy)**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **STP eToro %**

  ```
  SUM (IF [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) / COUNT([CID])
  ```

- **STP POA**

  ```
  if[POA IsResponseAutomatic]=1 and([POA_Manager]=0 or [POA_Manager]=Null) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **STP POI**

  ```
  if [POI IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POI_Manager]=0 or [POI_Manager]= NULL) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **STP prev month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then zn([Regular STP User %])+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **SUM Dep.Attempt**

  ```
  sum([DepositAttempt])
  ```

- **SUM FA**

  ```
  sum([FirstAction])
  ```

- **SUM FTD**

  ```
  SUM([Is FTD])
  ```

- **SUM Reg**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL0])
  ```

- **SUM Unverified FTD**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Is FTD] = 1 AND [IsVL3] = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **SUM VL1**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL1])
  ```

- **SUM VL2**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL2])
  ```

- **SUM VL3**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL3])
  ```

  ```
  sum([First Deposit Attempt in Reg Month (copy)])/count(CID)
  ```

- **sum([FTD in Reg Month])/sum([First Deposit Attempt in Reg Mon...**

  ```
  sum([FTD in Reg Month])/sum([First Deposit Attempt in Reg Month (copy)])
  ```

  ```
  sum([Is FTD])/count([CID])
  ```

  ```
  SUM([VL1 in Reg Month])/count([CID])
  ```

- **test 1**

  ```
  COUNTD([CID (copy)])/SUM([Total CID per month])
  ```

- **total**

  ```
  /*{FIXED [Period Ind VL2]:sum(if[Period Ind VL2] ='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)}/ {FIXED [Period Ind VL2]:COUNT([CID (copy)])}*/
  
   if[Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]='Curr
   Month' then { FIXED [Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]: sum(1)} else { FIXED [Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]: sum(0)} end
  ```

- **Total CID per month**

  ```
  { FIXED [Period Ind VL2] : COUNTD([CID (copy)]) }
  ```

- **VB: IsVL3<=72Hrs**

  ```
  IF [IsVL3] = 1
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 72
  THEN 'Yes' 
  ELSE 'No'
  END
  ```

- **VB: VL3 Categories**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 1
  THEN '<= 1 Hour'
  
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) > 1
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 24
  THEN '<= 24 Hrs'
  
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) > 24
  THEN '> 24 Hrs'
  
  ELSE 'Error Check'
  END
  ```

- **Verification Categories**

  ```
  IF     IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "Reg Only"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL1"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL2"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 1  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL3"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 1  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 1 THEN "Verified FTD"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 1 THEN "Unverified FTD"
  ELSE "Error In Flow"
  END
  ```

- **VL1 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL1]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL2 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL2]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL3 from reg  5 month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **VL3 from reg prev month diff abs **

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **VL3 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL3&FTD in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and year([DateTime FTD])=year([DateTime VL3]) 
    then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **WoW eToro STP % Change**

  ```
  COUNT(IF WEEK([DateTime VL3]) = WEEK(TODAY()) AND [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN CID END)
  /
  COUNT(IF WEEK([DateTime VL3]) = WEEK(DATEADD('week', -1, TODAY())) AND [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN CID END)
  -1
  ```

### Workbook: Onboarding Operations Excellence Report - Synapse

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (BI_DB)

- **Experienced Ind**

  ```
  IF[Experience_Level (group)]='Experienced' then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **sum([Q3_Is_Professional_Knowledge])/count([RealCID])**

  ```
  sum([Q3_Is_Professional_Knowledge])/count([RealCID])
  ```

#### Datasource: Operations Onboarding KPIs

- **% of VL3 < 1Hr**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **% of VL3 < 24Hr**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 24
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **% of VL3 > 3Day**

  ```
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) >= 72
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  /
  SUM(
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **%FA**

  ```
  [SUM FA]/[SUM Reg]
  ```

- **%STP POA**

  ```
  sum(if [POA IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POA_Manager]=0 or [POA_Manager]=Null) then 1 else 0 end)/count([CID])
  ```

- **%STP POI**

  ```
  sum(if[POI IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POI_Manager]=0 or [POI_Manager]=NULL) then 1 else 0 end )/count([CID])
  ```

- **%STP US**

  ```
  sum([Screening IsAutomatic])/count([CID])
  ```

  ```
  Before' then ([calc: Funded]/5) else [calc: Funded] end)
  ```

  ```
  Before' then ([DepositAttempt]/5) else [DepositAttempt] end)
  ```

- **calc: Funded**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **calc:#FA**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([FirstAction]/5) else [FirstAction] end)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL0]/5) else [IsVL0] end)
  ```

- **calc:#VL1**

  ```
  Before' then ([IsVL1]/5) else [IsVL1] end)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL2]/5) else [IsVL2] end)
  ```

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([IsVL3]/5) else [IsVL3] end)
  ```

- **calc:%Funded**

  ```
  sum([calc: Funded])/[SUM Reg]
  ```

- **calc:FTDs**

  ```
  sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then ([Is FTD]/5) else [Is FTD] end)
  ```

- **Docs Flow**

  ```
  IF [VD HasDocuments] = 0 THEN "No Docs"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 1 AND [POA IsApproved] = 1 THEN "Both Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 1 AND [POA IsApproved] = 0 THEN "POI Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 0 AND [POA IsApproved] = 1 THEN "POA Approved"
  ELSEIF [VD HasDocuments] = 1 AND [POI IsApproved] = 0 AND [POA IsApproved] = 0 THEN "Both Declined"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **Document SLA**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=2 then 'In 0-2 Minutes'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=10 then'In 3-10 minutes'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=180 then'11 min - 3 hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=360 then '4-6 Hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=720 then '7-12 Hours'
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('minute',[Max Document Upload Date],[Max Document Reviewed Date])<=1440 then '13-24 Hours'
  ELSE 'More then 24 Hours'
  end
  ```

- **Effected VL2 customers**

  ```
  SUM([IsVL2])
  ```

- **EV Flow**

  ```
  IF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND ISNULL([EV MatchStatusID]) THEN "EV: Not Sent"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND [EV MatchStatusID] IN (1, 2) THEN "EV: Verified"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 1 AND [EV MatchStatusID] IN (0, 3) THEN "EV: Not Verified"
  ELSEIF [EV IsCountryEligible] = 0 THEN "Non-EV"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **EV MatchStatus (copy)**

  ```
  [EV MatchStatus]
  ```

- **EV verified #**

  ```
  sum (if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]='Verified' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **EV verified or other verification**

  ```
  if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]='Verified' then 'EV'
   
   else 'Not sent to EV' end
  ```

- **EV vs. NonEv Category**

  ```
  IF IFNULL([EV MatchStatusID], 0) = 0 THEN "Not sent to EV"
  ELSEIF [EV MatchStatusID] IN (1, 2, 3) THEN "Sent to EV"
  END
  ```

- **FA in Reg Month (copy)**

  ```

  ELSEIF [DateTime FTD]>[DateTime VL3] then 'FTD After V3' 
  end
  ```

- **FTD EV Group**

  ```
  if [EV MatchStatus (copy)]<>'Verified' then 'Not Approved'
  elseif [FirstAction Ind]=1 then 'EV Approved+FA'
  elseif [FirstAction Ind]=0 then 'EV Approved+No FA'
  else 'Not Relevant' end
  ```

- **FTD in Reg Month**

  ```
  if  month([Date of Registration])=month([DateTime FTD]) 
  and year([Date of Registration])= year([DateTime FTD]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded and not Funded drill**

  ```
  IF [Funded FTD month]=1 then 'Funded - V3+FA'
  elseif [IsVL3]=1 then 'V3 No F.Action'
  ELSE 'No V3'
  end
  ```

- **Funded FTD month**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([FirstActionDate]) 
   and MONTH([DateTime FTD])>=MONTH([DateTime VL3])
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded FTD month (copy)**

  ```
  if [Is FTD]=1 and [IsVL3]=1 and [FirstAction]=1 and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([FirstActionDate]) 
   and MONTH([DateTime FTD])>=MONTH([DateTime VL3])
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Funded in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([FirstActionDate])   then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Non Verification Sub reason**

  ```
  if
  [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=0 and [POI IsApproved]=0 then 'Both Docs Not Approved'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=1 and [POI IsApproved]=0 then 'POI Not Approved'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Docs not Approved' and [POA IsApproved]=0 and [POI IsApproved]=1 then 'POA Not Approved'
  
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=0 and zn([POI IsApproved])=0 then 'Missing Both Docs'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=1 and zn([POI IsApproved])=0 then 'Missing POI'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='Missing Docs' and ZN([POA IsApproved])=0 and zn([POI IsApproved])=1 then 'Missing POA'
  
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='User Screening Issue' and ((ZN([POA IsApproved])=1 and zn([POI IsApproved])=1) or [EV MatchStatus]='Verified') and
  ([Phone Verification] ='AutomaticallyVerified' or [Phone Verification] ='ManualyVerified') then 'User Screening issue only'
  ELSEIF [NonVerificationReason]='User Screening Issue' then 'User Screening with other issues'
  
  else [NonVerificationReason]
  end
  ```

- **Not Funded Group (FTD Month)**

  ```
  IF [Funded FTD month]=0 and [IsVL3]=0 then 'No V3'
  elseif [Funded FTD month]=0 and [IsVL3]=1 and [DateTime VL3]<= [DateTime FTD] then 'V3 Before FTD + No FA'
  else 'V3 After FTD + No FA'
  end
  ```

- **Period Ind**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind (copy)**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 1.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind _Week**

  ```
  if [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) then 'Curr
   Week'
  elseif [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-14,TODAY()) then 'Prev
  Week'
    elseif [Date of Registration] >= dateadd('day',-70,TODAY()) then '8 Weeks
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind VL2**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[DateTime VL2],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **Period Ind_Summary**

  ```
  if DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 0.00 then 'This
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 1.00 then 'Curr
   Month'
  elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)= 2.00 then 'Prev
  Month'
   elseif DATEDIFF('month',[Date of Registration],TODAY()-1)> 2.00 then '5 Month
  Before'
  else 'Other Period'
  END
  ```

- **POA Decline Category**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([POA CountDeclines]) THEN "No Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] = 1 THEN "One Decline"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] IN (2, 3) THEN "2 to 3 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] IN (4, 5) THEN "4 to 5 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POA CountDeclines] > 5 THEN "More than 5 Declines"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **POI Decline Category**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([POI CountDeclines]) THEN "No Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] = 1 THEN "One Decline"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] IN (2, 3) THEN "2 to 3 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] IN (4, 5) THEN "4 to 5 Declines"
  ELSEIF [POI CountDeclines] > 5 THEN "More than 5 Declines"
  ELSE "Error"
  END
  ```

- **POI/POA STP User %**

  ```
  if [IsVL3] = 1
             and ([EV MatchStatus]='None' or isnull([EV MatchStatus])=TRUE 
                  )
             and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'     
             and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
             and [DateTime VL2]>DATE("2022-08-14")
  and [POA IsApproved]+[POI IsApproved]=2 and [POA_Manager]+[POI_Manager]=0
   
      then 1 
  end
  ```

- **Regular STP User %**

  ```
  IF [IsVL3] = 1 
           and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
           and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'
           and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
           and [Country ID]=219 
           and [Email Verification]=1
           THEN 1
       ELSEIF  [IsVL3] = 1 
               and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
               and ifnull([Screening Status],'NoMatch')='NoMatch'
               and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
               and [Designated Regulation]='CYSEC'
               and [Country ID]!=219 
               then 1 
      elseif [IsVL3] = 1
             and [EV MatchStatus]='Verified'
             and [Screening Status]='NoMatch'     
             and [Phone Verification]='AutomaticallyVerified'
             and [Country ID]!=219
      then 1  
  
       else 0 END
  ```

- **STP 5 month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then zn([Regular STP User %])+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **STP 5 month diff abs (copy)**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **STP eToro %**

  ```
  SUM (IF [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) / COUNT([CID])
  ```

- **STP POA**

  ```
  if[POA IsResponseAutomatic]=1 and([POA_Manager]=0 or [POA_Manager]=Null) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **STP POI**

  ```
  if [POI IsResponseAutomatic]>0 and ([POI_Manager]=0 or [POI_Manager]= NULL) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **STP prev month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then zn([Regular STP User %])+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then [Regular STP User %]+zn([POI/POA STP User %]) else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **total**

  ```
  /*{FIXED [Period Ind VL2]:sum(if[Period Ind VL2] ='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)}/ {FIXED [Period Ind VL2]:COUNT([CID (copy)])}*/
  
   if[Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]='Curr
   Month' then { FIXED [Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]: sum(1)} else { FIXED [Period Ind (copy 2)_611082180667727873]: sum(0)} end
  ```

- **Total CID per month**

  ```
  { FIXED [Period Ind VL2] : COUNTD([CID (copy)]) }
  ```

- **VB: IsVL3<=72Hrs**

  ```
  IF [IsVL3] = 1
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 72
  THEN 'Yes' 
  ELSE 'No'
  END
  ```

- **VB: VL3 Categories**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 1
  THEN '<= 1 Hour'
  
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) > 1
  AND DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) <= 24
  THEN '<= 24 Hrs'
  
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('hour', [DateTime VL0], [DateTime VL3]) > 24
  THEN '> 24 Hrs'
  
  ELSE 'Error Check'
  END
  ```

- **Verification Categories**

  ```
  IF     IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "Reg Only"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 0 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL1"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL2"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 1  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 0 THEN "In VL3"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 1  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 1 THEN "Verified FTD"
  ELSEIF IFNULL([IsVL0],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL1],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL2],0) = 1 AND IFNULL([IsVL3],0) = 0  AND IFNULL([Is FTD],0) = 1 THEN "Unverified FTD"
  ELSE "Error In Flow"
  END
  ```

- **VL1 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL1]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL2 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL2]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL3 from reg  5 month diff abs**

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='5 Month
  Before' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **VL3 from reg prev month diff abs **

  ```
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Curr
   Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  -
  
  sum (if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then [VL3 in Reg Month] else 0 end)/sum(if [Period Ind]='Prev
  Month' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **VL3 in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **VL3&FTD in Reg Month**

  ```
  if MONTH([Date of Registration])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and MONTH([DateTime FTD])=MONTH([DateTime VL3]) 
  and year([DateTime FTD])=year([DateTime VL3]) 
    then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **WoW eToro STP % Change**

  ```
  COUNT(IF WEEK([DateTime VL3]) = WEEK(TODAY()) AND [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN CID END)
  /
  COUNT(IF WEEK([DateTime VL3]) = WEEK(DATEADD('week', -1, TODAY())) AND [IsSTP eToro] = 1 THEN CID END)
  -1
  ```

### Workbook: Ticket Analysis -  Assigned to OPS

#### Datasource: TICKETS

- **# out of SLA**

  ```
  SUM(CASE [SLA] WHEN 'Out of SLA' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)
  ```

- **# solved **

  ```
  sum(case [Open/Closed TicketStatus] when 'Solved' then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **% In SLA**

  ```
  SUM(CASE [SLA] WHEN 'In SLA' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) /COUNT([CaseNumber])
  ```

- **% solved**

  ```
  sum(case [Open/Closed TicketStatus] when 'Solved' then 1 else 0 end)/count([CaseNumber])
  ```

- **%NoOfTouches>3**

  ```
  sum([NoOfTouches>3])/count([CaseNumber])
  ```

- **%Out of SLA **

  ```
  SUM(CASE [SLA] WHEN 'Out of SLA' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) /COUNT([CaseNumber])
  ```

- **Calculation1**

  ```
  (ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])) - LOOKUP(ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])), -1)) / ABS(LOOKUP(ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])), -1))
  ```

- **Calculation2**

  ```
  (ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])) - LOOKUP(ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])), -1)) / ABS(LOOKUP(ZN(COUNT([CaseNumber])), -1))
  ```

- **Calculation3**

  ```
  (ZN(AVG([NumberOfTouches])) - LOOKUP(ZN(AVG([NumberOfTouches])), -1)) / ABS(LOOKUP(ZN(AVG([NumberOfTouches])), -1))
  ```

- **Calculation4**

  ```
  (ZN(AVG([LastCsat])) - LOOKUP(ZN(AVG([LastCsat])), -1)) / ABS(LOOKUP(ZN(AVG([LastCsat])), -1))
  ```

- **CO tickets opened/Total CO**

  ```
  count([CaseNumber])/count([federated.199yz4d0y7idg812s4qha1f5fc9c].[WithdrawID])
  ```

- **exclude curren week**

  ```
  if ISOWEEK([CreatedDate])=ISOWEEK(today()) then 0 else 1 end
  ```

- **Exclude current month**

  ```
  if DATEPART('month', [CreatedDate]) = DATEPART('month', today())
  and 
  DATEPART('year', [CreatedDate]) = DATEPART('year', today())
   then 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **NoOfTouches>3**

  ```
  if [NumberOfTouches]>3 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Number of Touches calculation**

  ```
  lookup(MAX(([NumberOfTouches])),0)
  ```

- **NumberOfTouches calculation**

  ```
  lookup(MAX(([NumberOfTouches])),0)
  ```

- **SubType (copy)**

  ```
  [SubType]
  ```

- **Wire tickets opened/Total Wires**

  ```
  count([CaseNumber])/count([federated.1wu0q3g1drdvyx1ajrl860dnuzbe].[DepositID])
  ```

#### Datasource: verifications level 2

- **TotalTickets/TotalLevel2**

  ```
  count([federated.0t4iev10nwu4kh12is5bw1haffmr].[CaseNumber])/count([CID])
  ```
