- **This Week Filter**

  ```
  if [This Week] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Week old**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY())) <= [FullDate] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Year**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [FullDate] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[FullDate],TODAY()) = 1 then [Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday **

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

#### Datasource: DailyCommissionReport CID Level

- **2 Days Ago**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 2 then [Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Accumulated %**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Yesterday])) / TOTAL(SUM([Yesterday]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks])) / TOTAL(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Last Month Same Time])) / TOTAL(SUM([Last Month Same Time]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % This Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([This Month])) / TOTAL(SUM([This Month]))
  ```

- **ADF**

  ```
  if [Filter Applicationers Only?] = "Yes" then ATTR([ProfessionalApplicationDate])
  ELSE #2001-01-01# end
   >= if [Filter Applicationers Only?] = "Yes" then [Application Date Parameter]
  else #2000-01-01# END
  ```

- **Avg 8 Last Weeks Groups **

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 200 then 200
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 300 then 300
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 400 then 400
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] >= 5000 then 5001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg Day This Year**

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **Avg Last 8 Weeks Filter**

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg per Day This Year**

  ```
  sum(if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end)
  /
  sum(if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **check**

  ```
  if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Contribution to Comm.**

  ```
  if [Accumulated %] < 0.1 then '10% of Comm' 
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.2 then '20% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.3 then '30% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.4 then '40% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.5 then '50% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.99 then '99% of Comm'
  else '100% of Comm'
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Filter**

  ```
  if [Last Month Same Time] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time**

  ```
  if day([Full Date])<day(today()) and MONTH([Full Date])+1=MONTH(today()) and year([Full Date]) = year(TODAY())
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Groups**

  ```
  if [Last Month Same Time] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [Last Month Same Time] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [Last Month Same Time] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 2000 then 2000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 20000 then 20000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] >= 20000 then 20001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Number of Records**

  ```
  1
  ```

- **Rank**

  ```
  RANK( sum([Yesterday]),'desc')
  ```

- **Same DayWeek **

  ```
  'Last 8 weeks Top20'
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [Commissions]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **Test**

  ```
  [This Month Groups]
  ```

- **This Month**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('month',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Month **

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **This Month Filter**

  ```
  if [This Month] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Month Groups**

  ```
  if sum([This Month]) < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF sum([This Month]) < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF sum([This Month]) < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 2000 then 2000
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) < 20000 then 20000
  ELSEIF  sum([This Month]) >= 20000 then 20001
  else 0
  end
  ```

  else 0
  end

  end

- **Yesterday Commission in risk  **

  ```

  end
  ```

- **Yesterday Filter**

  ```
  if [Yesterday] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday Groups**

  ```
  if [Yesterday] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [Yesterday] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [Yesterday] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 200 then 200
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 300 then 300
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 400 then 400
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [Yesterday] >= 5000 then 5001
  else 0
  end
  ```
